Washington Conference

Japan Plans to Seize the Opportunity to Employ Diplomatic Maneuvers 24

Will Persuade the United States to Abandon the Stimson Doctrine

Hoping to Obtain Economic Assistance

Ishii's Name is Most Often Mentioned as Representative

(Tokyo) The Japanese delegation participating in the London World Economic Conference and the preliminary talks in Washington will depart for Washington in mid-May. Finance Minister Takahashi, Interior Minister Yamamoto, and Privy Councilor Ishii have all been mentioned as possible representatives. Takahashi and Yamamoto are unlikely to leave Japan, so Ishii is the most promising. (11th Reuters Telegram)

(Tokyo) The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs considers Roosevelt's proposal for a preliminary meeting to be an excellent opportunity to break through its isolated diplomacy after withdrawing from the League of Nations. It held a ministry meeting yesterday afternoon to decide on the basic countermeasures as follows: (1) Regarding the World Economic Conference, the Japanese government considers it an important opportunity. Foreign Minister Uchida will report on the details of the process at the cabinet meeting on the 11th. The representative must be selected from among ministers. (2) Finance Minister Takahashi is the most suitable person to be the Japanese representative. If Takahashi firmly declines due to illness, he should not be forced to accept. However, the selection of the representative must be made by the cabinet to avoid political turmoil. (3) This meeting is for individual contacts. The Japanese representative's contact with Roosevelt is scheduled for late May, so there is plenty of time. The Japanese government must take this opportunity to explain to the US President the truth about Japan's policy towards Manchuria, persuade Roosevelt to abandon the Stimson Doctrine, and discuss the basic principles of the naval disarmament conference to be held in 1936. Therefore, the Foreign Ministry's intended representatives are Viscount Kikujiro Ishii or Baron Kijuro Shidehara, former Foreign Minister. Shidehara has succumbed to the military since the September 18th Incident and should have his talents re-employed at this opportunity. (11th China United Press Telegram)

(Tokyo) The Japanese cabinet held a cabinet meeting at 10:00 this morning, where Foreign Minister Uchida reported on the contents of the invitation to the World Economic Conference. Three items were discussed on the spot: (1) Attendance, yes or no; (2) Representative selection; (3) What are the countermeasures? For the first item, due to the current state of the Japanese economy's need for world cooperation and assistance, and as it is the only opportunity to cooperate with the world after withdrawing from the League of Nations, it was decided to participate. As for the representatives and the outline of policy towards China, it was entrusted to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to handle, and then a meeting of the five ministers of Foreign Affairs, Finance, Commerce and Industry, Agriculture and Forestry, and Colonial Affairs will be held to formulate principles and select several plenipotentiary representatives, which will then be submitted to the cabinet for approval, and finally Foreign Minister Uchida will reply to the US State Department. (11th China United Press Telegram)

(Tokyo) The Japanese financial community believes that the Washington preliminary meeting is crucial to Japan's future. The economic foundation for invading China after the September 18th Incident cannot be established without foreign capital. Given the current diplomatic situation, it is impossible to seek help from foreign countries. Therefore, many influential figures in the financial community advocate taking the opportunity to send representatives to the United States to seek Roosevelt's understanding. If the United States is willing to assist Japan, its policy towards Manchuria will not fail, and the domestic economy can also escape from a dangerous environment. The proposed representatives from the financial community are rumored to be Kenkichi Kagemi, representative of the Mitsubishi zaibatsu, or Baron Seinosuke Gō, representative of the Mitsui zaibatsu, but neither has formally agreed. (11th China United Press Telegram)

Hull and the British Ambassador Discuss Silver Issues 31

European Debtor Nations Form a United Front 32

(Washington) Yesterday, rumors spread here that European debtor nations will form their own united front to request the US government to allow a delay in the payment of war debts due on June 15 until the end of the World Economic Conference. The representatives of Britain, France, Italy, and other debtor nations, who are about to arrive here, will submit the above request to the US government. Government officials said that President Roosevelt would certainly reject this approach, and that the leaders of both the Democratic and Republican parties in Congress also oppose it. The principal of the war debts due amounts to $41,153,840, and the interest amounts to $103,026,834. If some debtor nations cannot obtain permission to postpone payment, they will request an extension of the repayment of the principal. If notice is given within 90 days before the due date, the US Treasury Department can approve it without waiting for congressional approval, but President Roosevelt also opposes this. Roosevelt's intention is to first know whether European countries are prepared to make commercial concessions, and then he will agree to negotiate on the war debt issue. (10th Havas Telegram)

The Sino-Eastern Railway Dispute Escalates, and a Dangerous Situation Arises Between Russia and Japan 34

Japan Incites Puppet Organizations to Cut Off the Eastern Railway's Connection to Provoke Russia

Railway Tracks are Demolished; Rumor is that Japanese and Puppet Troops are Moving Towards the Russian Border

Reports of Banditry are Frequent in the Eastern Section of the Sino-Eastern Railway; Japanese Intentions are Unpredictable

(Changchun) Due to the Sino-Eastern Railway issue, a dangerous situation has arisen between Russia and Japan. The government has repeatedly incited puppet organizations to cut off the Sino-Eastern Railway's connection. The Soviet Union is fully aware that Japan intends to provoke and make unreasonable demands. Since April 8, it has begun to retaliate. International trains are being rerouted through the Ussuri Railway. The Sino-Eastern Railway refuses to transport munitions and military supplies. The Japanese army has been actively transporting large quantities of military supplies to major military locations in the Suifenhe and Manzhouli areas over the past month, preparing to attack the Soviet Union, but this has been fully exposed by the Soviet Union. As a result, disputes are becoming increasingly fierce. The South Manchuria Railway has decided to set up a railway sub-bureau in Harbin to exclusively handle matters related to the Sino-Eastern Railway, in order to seize the Sino-Eastern Railway. It will begin operations within days. (11th China United Press Telegram)

(Harbin) The situation regarding the dispute between the Soviet Union and "Manchukuo" over the Chinese Eastern Railway is becoming increasingly serious. The switches on the western section of the Chinese Eastern Railway were all removed today, and several dozen yards of railway tracks were demolished. "Manchukuo" troops are currently stationed in the square near the railway office, preparing to respond to the incident. Rumors are spreading that Japanese reinforcements have now moved west from Qiqihar. The "Manchukuo" Foreign Ministry yesterday sent a note to Soviet Consul General Slavutsky, requesting that all Soviet customs personnel in Manzhouli and Suifenhe leave their posts. (11th Reuters Telegram)

(Harbin) Regarding the events that occurred in Manchuria yesterday morning, it seems that a serious railway dispute is likely to occur between "Manchukuo" and Russia. Yesterday, the Japanese military authorities declared that they would use their own personnel to maintain the Chinese Eastern Railway's train operations. This dispute arose from the Chinese Eastern Railway Bureau's refusal to allow trains between Manzhouli and Harbin to run to and from Siberia. The railway bureau's action was taken on the orders of Rudy, the Russian director of the Chinese Eastern Railway, and Rudy issued this order because the "Manchukuo" authorities and police cut off the connection between Outer Baikal and the Chinese Eastern Railway, and so he made this retaliatory action.

Trains Cannot Pass Through Manchurian Territory 35

After several hours of negotiations yesterday, a train from Manzhouli departed for Harbin, but it was detained after reaching the Dihuiqi station. After several hours, it returned to Manzhouli. Finally, the Japanese military authorities warned the railway bureau that if the trains did not run, the Japanese army would use its own personnel to maintain traffic. Therefore, the train resumed running. The two roads in the eastern border of Suifenhe are also not connected, so that trains cannot now enter or leave Manchurian territory.

Japanese Newspaper Advocates for Rudy's Dismissal 36

At the same time, the Harbin Times, a Japanese newspaper that is regarded as the official organ of the Japanese, published an article today demanding the dismissal of Rudy, pointing to him as the person responsible for moving the Chinese Eastern Railway Bureau's vehicles into Russian territory. It said that the Chinese Eastern Railway's Russian employees spontaneously moved 75 locomotives, 739 passenger cars, and approximately 4,000 freight cars into Russian territory. In addition, Su Bingwen also moved 27 locomotives and 250 passenger cars. It was found that the departure of these vehicles was due to Rudy's special orders. Therefore, it is now appropriate to detain him and interrogate him. Rudy has secretly moved vehicles without authorization, and recently there has been a conspiracy to transport locomotives out of Manzhouli. His actions are no different from stealing in the night.

A Small Spark Can Start a Prairie Fire 37

When Moscow is preparing to conclude a non-aggression pact with Japan, Rudy is actually stealing vehicles. This not only violates the principle of shared ownership of the Chinese Eastern Railway and its business, but will also lead to war between Russia and Japan. A small spark can start a prairie fire. To prevent this in advance, the administration of the Chinese Eastern Railway Bureau must be reformed immediately. But if those who are playing with fire are not removed immediately, bystanders will also suffer the disaster of being burned. If Moscow really wants to maintain peace with Japan, just as Tokyo wants to maintain peace with Russia, then why not dismiss Rudy, because he is now trying his best to destroy the possibility of Russian-Japanese friendship and to incite conflict between the two countries? The Russian employees of the Chinese Eastern Railway must also know that Rudy's dangerous actions will have very harmful consequences, not just burning their hands. (11th Reuters Telegram)

Who is Really Behind the Rampant Banditry? 38

(Moscow) News from Suifenhe says that the eastern section of the Chinese Eastern Railway is now in a dangerous state. Bandits are constantly attacking stations, destroying railway tracks, and kidnapping and killing residents. For example, on March 11, a train was shot and destroyed by bandits on the Badashiz section. When such situations occur, the railway police are often not on the scene, or arrive too late. In fact, there is no protection at all for the railway's employees and property. The bandits' ability to escape safely and their increasingly escalating behavior are said to be due to their close relationship with the "Manchukuo" authorities and certain Japanese elements. The latter's purpose is to paralyze traffic on the section of the Chinese Eastern Railway to Vladivostok by all means. The Japanese and "Manchukuo" newspapers in Harbin have begun an anti-Soviet provocation campaign, falsely accusing the Soviet authorities of aiding the anti-"Manchukuo" forces in the eastern section of the Chinese Eastern Railway. It is reported that, at the instigation of certain Japanese elements, White Russians will again arrest a large number of Soviet people serving in the eastern section of the Chinese Eastern Railway, falsely accusing them of colluding with bandits. (10th TASS Telegram)

(Moscow) Today, Soviet officials predict that a large number of Russian employees of the Chinese Eastern Railway will be arrested, as reports from Boli in recent days indicate that there have been many incidents of banditry in the eastern section of the Chinese Eastern Railway. Many people have been killed there, and several Russian railway employees have been kidnapped for ransom. It seems that these actions by the bandits have been secretly instructed by the authorities, and that the list of those kidnapped has also been drawn up in advance. At present, there are widespread rumors in northern Manchuria that Soviet railway employees are secretly assisting anti-Manchu forces. This statement is baseless and seems to be deliberately spread by the authorities in order to provide a pretext for mass arrests. Furthermore, officials in Boli have repeatedly reported that there is a clear understanding between the bandits and the "Manchukuo" puppet officials in the eastern section of the Chinese Eastern Railway. Therefore, bandits have repeatedly destroyed railway property, and the authorities have not stopped them, because their intention is to obstruct transportation between northern Manchuria and Vladivostok. The telegram also stated that the White Russian railway protection troops have even colluded with the bandits to carry out their sabotage plans. (10th National Telegram)

Japan Cunningly Conceals Itself Behind the Scenes 39

(Nanjing) Japanese official circles consider the dispute over the Chinese Eastern Railway as merely an event between "Manchukuo" and Soviet Russia. British Boxer Indemnity and Railways 45

British Foreign Secretary Explains in Parliament

(London) During today's session of the House of Commons, Conservative Party Member of Parliament Walter Runciman asked the Foreign Secretary whether he would notify the Chinese government regarding the lending of British Boxer Indemnity funds to Chinese railways, only to the extent that there were established methods for clearing previous debts on the railways. Foreign Secretary Simon replied that rectifying and completing existing railways would be sufficient to increase the revenue of such railways, and thereby improve the position of those holding bonds secured by such railways. The policy proposed by Walter would have the opposite effect, as it would prevent any particular railway from borrowing funds to increase its revenue, and without such funds, its revenue would still be insufficient to cover ordinary expenses. (Reuter, 10th)

The Focus of the European Situation: Italian-German-Austrian "Roman Talks" 69

Papen and Göring Meet with the Pope and Mussolini

Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss Also Rushes to Arrive by Plane

Hitler Prepares to Go to Rome

Reuter, Rome, 10th German Vice-Chancellor Papen held his first meeting with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini today to discuss the Four-Power Pact and other matters. The Italian Prime Minister will meet with German Reichstag President Göring tomorrow. Göring came here to assist Papen in the discussions. The Italian Prime Minister also met with the French Ambassador today. It is heard that the French Ambassador has submitted a memorandum regarding the Four-Power Plan to the Italian Prime Minister. Göring spoke with the Pope's Secretary of State for an hour today and will probably be received by the Pope on Wednesday. It is heard that German Chancellor Hitler has now gone to Bavaria to spend his Easter holiday, but if Göring believes it is necessary for Hitler to come to Rome in person, then Hitler is prepared to come here. From this, it can be seen that the Roman discussions are very important.

National Telegram, Rome, 10th After arriving here today, German Vice-Chancellor Papen expressed to Italian journalists his feelings of gratitude for the welcome given by Italy. He also said that this meeting with the Italian Prime Minister will definitely enhance the friendship between the two countries. The Italian newspapers are all using

Lengthy articles praising Hitler's achievements in unifying Germany. German Reichstag President Göring flew here from Munich at noon today. The Italian Minister of Aviation and the German Ambassador and others went to greet him. Papen paid a visit to Italian Prime Minister Mussolini this afternoon for an hour-long meeting. Mussolini expressed deep goodwill. National Telegram, Rome, 11th German Vice-Chancellor Papen will be received by the Pope tomorrow evening. Political circles here are paying close attention to this move. Papen is a devout Catholic, and Hitler chose him as his representative. The Vatican regards it as an act of respect.

Austrian Chancellor Arrives in Rome 70

National Telegram, Vienna, 10th The official announcement stated that Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss will fly to Rome tomorrow to participate in the Easter ceremony and will visit Italian Prime Minister Mussolini. German Vice-Chancellor Papen and Cabinet Member Göring have already arrived in Rome. Now Dollfuss has followed, so the public is paying close attention to this move. Political circles here generally expect that there will be important developments in Rome this week.

Havas, Vienna, 11th Chancellor Dollfuss departed by plane for Rome at 11:15 this morning. The press has unanimously expressed surprise at the Chancellor's trip, saying that it contains significant political meaning. The Neue Freie Presse said that the Chancellor's trip has no special significance, as the Chancellor has repeatedly pointed out that Austria's policy is by no means opposed to any country. The Neue Wiener Tagblatt said that after Italian Prime Minister Mussolini talked with German politicians, he very much wanted to know the opinions of Austrian political leaders, so the Austrian Chancellor made this trip. The Arbeiter-Zeitung argued that the Parliamentary Principles Committee should convene immediately to ask Dollfuss to explain the reasons for his sudden trip to Italy.

France Submits Memorandum to Britain and Italy 71

National Telegram, Paris, 10th France's counterproposal to the Four-Power Pact was submitted to the British and Italian governments today. The counterproposal is in the form of a memorandum, only two pages long, and also includes a cover letter. The views of the French government stated therein are similar to those stated by French Premier Daladier in his speech the other day. The memorandum is not intended to be made public. It is only known that France's opinion is that the French government has already recognized the principle of four-country cooperation, but this cooperation must first comply with the provisions of the League of Nations Covenant, especially Articles 10, 11, 12, 15, 16, and 19. These articles concern the territorial integrity of member states of the League of Nations, arbitration, and the modification of treaties. It is generally said that the memorandum submitted by France this time amounts to an implicit rejection of Italian Prime Minister Mussolini's plan, but it is quite noteworthy that it actually proposes the possibility of modifying the treaty.

Göring Appointed Prime Minister of Prussia 72

Havas, Berlin, 11th Chancellor Hitler, in his capacity as the concurrent Governor of Prussia, appointed the current Prussian Minister of Interior Göring as the Prussian Prime Minister. This decision has been telegraphed to Göring in Rome. Since the dismissal of the Social Democratic Blum government of Prussia on July 20 last year, a federal special administrative commissioner has been governing it. With this appointment, the special administrative commissioner system has come to an end.

Havas, Berlin, 11th After the changes in the German local system, the original seventeen states and free cities have only ten governors' offices. The free cities of Bremen, Hamburg, and Lübeck have only one governor's office. The three parts of Oldenburg, Lippe-Detmold, and Schaumburg-Lippe have a total of one governor's office.

German-Polish Relations Worsen 73

National Telegram, Berlin, 10th The German government has recently instructed its minister in Warsaw to lodge a strong protest with the Polish government regarding the anti-German demonstrations and various acts of impropriety prevalent throughout Poland. In its protest, Germany demanded that those who incite the anti-German movement be punished, and that every effort be made to protect German consulates throughout the region.

Franco-Turkish Debt Agreement Concluded 74

Havas, Paris, 11th Foreign Minister Pengu met with Turkish Ambassador to France Suad and French Ambassador to Turkey Shampron this morning to discuss the Turkish debt agreement. The agreement was initialed yesterday.

The Soviet Court Procedure 75

Reuter, Moscow, 10th The trial of the six British engineers of the Vickers company accused of espionage is scheduled to begin on Wednesday at noon. The public is paying close attention to this case, and almost everyone wants to obtain a spectator ticket, so the authorities are issuing these tickets very carefully. The trial venue is the Trade Union Hall, formerly known as the Blue Room, now renamed the October Hall, which can accommodate 500 people. This hall is connected to another room where Lenin's remains were previously displayed. The judges and defendants are allowed to smoke during the trial. There is a tea and snack room next to the courtroom where non-intoxicating beverages are available. During the trial, the defendants are surrounded by Red Guards. There is a light in the courtroom that shines directly on the faces of the defendants. This is a special arrangement for the court. The Russian authorities warned the defendants today not to discuss their cases with their fellow countrymen who have come to observe the trial. Britain will send representatives to attend the trial. The Russian government and the Communist Party's newspapers today published impassioned criticisms of the British government's proposed restrictions on imports of Russian goods.

Luan East Counter-Offensive: Enemy Troops Routed to 76

Recapture Haiyang and Liujiang, and Advance Straight to Shimen

Small-Scale Contacts Also Occur From Time to Time at Various Passes Along the Great Wall

Special Dispatch from Beiping After the Beiping military conference, the Luan East defenses were reorganized, and subsequent reinforcements were rushed to the front lines, boosting morale greatly. On the 7th, a full-scale counter-offensive was launched, with He Zhuguo also personally going to the front to command. After fierce fighting throughout the day, Haiyangzhen [Haiyang Town] was recaptured.

Advance towards Dawangzhuang, advance north along Liujiang Road, and encircle from the left and right wings, advancing directly to Shimen Village. The enemy forces could not withstand the pressure and retreated in disarray. In the past two days, the fighting has been increasingly smooth, and a siege of Shimen has already been established. At the same time, on the Jielingkou front, our troops have also increased their forces to prevent the enemy from circumventing the attack. On the Gubei, Xifeng, and Lengkou fronts, defensive offensives have been launched in coordination with the various armies in Luan East. The war situation on each route is recorded separately below.

Enemy Offensive Strategy 77

In their military operations, the Japanese army avoids reality and attacks the void, adopting a strategy of surprise attacks. After the failure of the attacks on Xifengkou and Lengkou, they realized that our forces in that area were strong and did not dare to confront them directly. Instead, they turned towards Luan East, attempting to take advantage of the opportunity to penetrate deeply, disturbing our rear. If Luan East is shaken, the various passes of the Great Wall will lose their natural barriers and be difficult to defend. Our army saw through their conspiracy, and while defending the various passes, it also transferred a large army to reinforce Luan East, taking an encirclement strategy against the enemy forces that had invaded Shimen Village. Therefore, since the reorganization of the Luan East defenses, a fierce counter-offensive has been launched, and the enemy has retreated in disarray.

Great Victory in the Counteroffensive in Luandong 78

Our troops in Luandong launched a full-scale counteroffensive at dawn on the 7th. On the Tang River front, they crossed Da Wangzhuang. Haiyang was also recovered by our Zhang and Tian regiments. The enemy troops retreated to Liujiang. On the 8th, our main force advanced along the Liujiang road, fiercely attacking Liujiang Station. The left and right wings, from the area of Da Wangzhuang, Yaozhouzhai, and Taipingzhuang, outflanked the enemy's rear, directly threatening Shimentouzhai. After a day of fierce fighting, they recovered various locations west of Da Wangzhuang and villages such as Zhao Zhuang, Xin Zhuang, and Yang Chang. The vanguard reached a point ten miles from Shimentouzhai. On the night of the 8th, all forces advanced towards Shimentouzhai, forming an encirclement. It is widely rumored today that our troops captured Shimentouzhai last night (the 8th), but as of press time, there has been no official telegram to confirm this. The enemy troops invading Luandong this time include over 2,000 Japanese soldiers and over 4,000 puppet troops, as well as organized plainclothes teams infiltrating and disrupting our positions. In terms of weaponry, they have over 20 aircraft and 30 tanks and armored vehicles. In terms of weaponry, our troops are undoubtedly inferior. However, in terms of troop quality, our troops are superior. Since receiving reinforcements of infantry, cavalry, and artillery, our troops have been emboldened and have successively recovered lost territory. The enemy troops are retreating in disarray, and many have been captured. According to a telegram from Luanzhou this afternoon (the 9th), the remnants of the enemy troops have retreated and gathered at Shimentouzhai, numbering approximately 4,000. They are currently building strong fortifications near Shimentouzhai to defend against our attack and await reinforcements. A train carrying Japanese soldiers arrived this morning and has turned towards Jiumentou. The Kwantung Army headquarters, having received news of the Japanese defeat, has transferred Japanese troops stationed in Jinzhou westward, indicating a possible large-scale invasion again. This morning, three enemy aircraft flew over the Haiyangzhen Tang River area for reconnaissance and bombing. One reconnaissance plane also arrived over Luanzhou. Based on the current situation, although the Japanese troops have been defeated, they have not abandoned their attempt to invade and harass Luandong. Our troops are also determined to capture Shimentouzhai. It is expected that a large-scale main force battle will occur within the next few days.

Battle Situation at Various Passes of the Great Wall 79

After the Japanese troops' invasion of Luandong was thwarted, they continued to harass various passes of the Great Wall in an attempt to contain our forces. There have been minor skirmishes in the areas of Xifengkou, Lengkou, and Jielingkou in recent days. On the 7th, the enemy troops on the Xifengkou front, under the cover of intense artillery fire, attacked our Laopashan and Haierling areas. After a day of fierce fighting, our Zhao and Huang brigades launched flanking attacks on the enemy, killing many enemy troops by 12:00 AM. The enemy forces, unable to withstand the attack, retreated. Our troops also suffered considerable losses. At dawn on the 8th, the Japanese troops increased their forces and launched a counterattack. The artillery fire was extremely intense. Our troops resolutely fought back and eventually repelled the Japanese troops. Yesterday morning (the 8th) from 7:00 AM to 12:00 PM, five Japanese aircraft flew to the Santunying and Saheqiao areas, dropping heavy bombs, causing dozens of casualties among soldiers and civilians. Today (the 9th), there are still Japanese troops harassing outside Xifengkou. On the Lengkou front, on the morning of the 7th, approximately 300 to 400 Japanese soldiers bypassed Dongjiakou and approached Lengkou. Our troops immediately launched a fierce attack. After a standoff until the afternoon, the enemy retreated to Beishuiyuzhuang, where they built fortifications in an attempt to resist. Our troops have launched an attack forward from Taipingzhai. Our troops stationed at Madaogou also clashed with Japanese sentries on the evening of the 7th. The enemy was repelled. Yesterday, three Japanese aircraft bombed Jianchangyingzi, Lengkou, and other places extensively. Our troops had taken precautions and hidden in concealed locations, so there was no significant damage. On the Jielingkou front, over 300 Japanese soldiers advanced towards our positions from Wangjiagou and Liushugou at dawn on the 7th and were repelled by our troops. The enemy in that area is reinforcing troops and appears to be preparing to attack us. Our troops have now reinforced the area, and the defenses are extremely solid. The Japanese troops' continuous harassment of various passes of the Great Wall is disruptive in nature and intended to contain our forces. There will likely be no large-scale fierce battles for the time being.

Atrocities of Japanese Troops on the Front Lines 80

According to a telegram from He Zhuguo at 7:00 PM on the 7th, Sergeant Hou □□ of the □ Regiment, who was unable to retreat during the Shimentouzhai battle, disguised himself as a civilian and was taken by the Japanese troops to serve as a porter. He escaped during a Japanese retreat. According to him, the Japanese troops treat our civilians as less than human, with extremely brutal treatment. They are not given enough to eat each day, and when they rest, they are imprisoned in a room. Any slight dissatisfaction results in beatings with fists, feet, and gun butts, and some are even shot to death. During the Shimentouzhai battle, he witnessed over 300 enemy casualties, including eight officers, one of whom was a junior officer named Kojima Kotaro, whose rank is unknown. There were also over 70 corpses. The puppet government officials suffered even more casualties. Over 30 political officers from Ding Qiang's (Li Jichun's) unit were casualties at Qianshuiying, leaving only about a dozen survivors. According to reports from plainclothes scouts sent by our troops outside the Great Wall, the Japanese troops are committing all kinds of atrocities in the villages within the territory of Rehe and the Hebei border area outside the Great Wall. Under the pretext of searching for guerrillas, they forcibly take away livestock from civilian homes, such as cattle, sheep, chickens, and ducks. The people in those areas, who depend on cattle and sheep for their livelihoods, are filled with resentment and despair upon seeing this. Many men flee into the mountains and attack and kill Japanese troops in an attempt to retaliate. Many women have committed suicide after being raped by Japanese troops. Particularly tragic is the case of a Chinese woman who was shot to death for arguing with Japanese soldiers who tried to take her beef without paying and crying loudly. Several pregnant women were also stabbed to death by Japanese soldiers with bayonets through their abdomens. The atrocities are too terrible to describe. (April 9th)

Important Military Conference to Be Held in Nanchang 81

Military and Political Leaders from Various Provinces Arrive in Jiangxi One After Another

Central Theme Focuses on Resisting Japan and Suppressing Bandits

Nanchang Dispatch: In order to coordinate the military affairs of resisting Japan and suppressing the Red Army, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek has convened a meeting of senior officials from various provinces in Jiangxi. Those who have already arrived in Jiangxi include Zhu Shaoliang, Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in the Hunan-Hubei-Jiangxi Border Area; Xu Yuanquan, Hubei Rural Pacification Commissioner; Shangguan Yunxiang, Commander of the 54th Division; Liu Zhi, Chairman of Henan Province; Yang Hucheng, Chairman of Shaanxi Province; Liu Zhenhua, Commander-in-Chief of the 11th Route Army; Wang Jun, Commander of the 3rd Army and Commander of the Tianjin-Pukou Railway Garrison; Liang Guanying, Commander-in-Chief of the 25th Route Army; Yang Yongtai, Secretary-General of the Headquarters of the Three Provinces; Gu Zhutong, Chairman of Jiangsu Province; Yu Jishi, Director of Security of Zhejiang Province; Zhang Fang, Commander-in-Chief of the 20th Route Army; Shao Lizi, Chairman of Gansu Province; and Jiang Dingwen, Director of the Yangtze River Water Police Bureau. Those who have telegraphed their departure include Huang Shaohong, Minister of the Interior, and senior military officers from the Military Affairs Commission and the Ministry of War, as well as other military and political leaders from various provinces. The headquarters has set up reception centers at No. 3 Gongyuan Back Street and the Jiangxi Grand Hotel. It is reported that Chiang Kai-shek will convene the conference after all the generals have arrived to discuss the most important issues: (1) National defense arrangements; (2) Mobilizing elite troops from various provinces to participate in the war against Japan; (3) Coordinating bandit suppression among various provinces to achieve early pacification; (4) Arrangements for public security and coastal defense along the Yangtze River in various provinces during the war against Japan and bandit suppression; (5) Clearing the Red Army from the southeastern provinces in a short period of time so that the bandit suppression forces can be transferred to resist Japan; (6) Reorganizing, training, and providing salaries for the troops stationed in various provinces. According to Liu Zhi, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek has summoned senior generals to Jiangxi to discuss plans for bandit suppression in various provinces. The duration of the conference will be determined after all the generals have arrived. (April 9th)

Uprising of Villagers in Lin'an, Zhejiang 82

The Uprising Area Almost Covers the Entire City

Losses Estimated at Over 90,000 Yuan

The Steps Seem to Have a Strict Plan

It Seems That There Are People Initiating the Uprising Behind the Scenes

Hangzhou Dispatch: A group of people in Lin'an County recently misunderstand the improved silkworm seeds and causes a big riot. It burns down all kinds of seed farms. According to rumors, the inside story of this matter is very noteworthy. The command and planning are very strict. It doesn't seem like an ordinary case. Here are the details of the investigation, especially noted below:

On the fifth of this month, the Fourth District Office sent personnel to Lingfeng Township to collect local silkworm seeds. Tang Laoer, a villager in the township, was the first to object and beat up the basic team. The next day, District Chief Pan Jiong Rong personally went to persuade them. When Pan arrived at the township, □□□ and others had already gathered two or three hundred villagers, and closed Pan in the Tang Family Ancestral Hall, asking to raise local silkworm seeds and defeat foreign seeds. Seeing the crowd surging, Pan immediately agreed in order to avoid causing trouble. Then he asked Pan to issue a notice, and he also agreed. Then he asked Pan to issue a guarantee, and he also agreed. Just as the voices were noisy, suddenly □□□ led two or three hundred villagers from Jinshi Township and Fuxing Township to arrive and broke into the Tang Family Ancestral Hall and joined in the coercion. Pan had to pay a deposit of 500 yuan. Pan could not pay the cash and promised to issue a voucher. At that time, the villager Xu Jinquan did not think it was right, saying that even if the guarantee voucher was issued, where would it be received? He was immediately scolded and beaten by the crowd, and a woman nicknamed Jiu Huaniang bit Xu's legs twice. Pan persuaded and beat Pan again. After being protected by emotionally related person, he was pushed into a small house and was spared serious injury. Later, the villagers asked Pan to pay sixty yuan for the meal, and took Pan to the county for a petition. When passing through Jinxiang Township, Pan paid 15 yuan to buy sesame cakes for food. After eating, he rang the gong in the township and shouted loudly, forcing the villagers of the township to enter the city together to petition, otherwise the houses in the township would be burned. The county party and government organs heard about it, and decided to send Pan Qi, a member of the Standing Committee of the County Party Committee, to explain and dissuade the city. When the party committee set off to a place near Shili Langbi, he explained to the leader □□□ and pleaded bitterly with the public. As a result, he was scolded and returned without success. The crowd then gathered in front of the stage outside the Xiangmen Gate of the county seat. At that time, county party committee members Pan Qi, Hu Gezhen, and local gentry Zhou Zigong and others went to persuade the villagers as much as possible. The villagers did not listen and made many demands. In order to avoid the expansion of the storm, the county government prepared a notice to ban the crackdown on the local silkworm seeds. Then, the villagers went to the Xihu Seed Breeding Farm, first destroying the three-story foreign house of the seed farm, then pouring kerosene and setting fire, and monitoring the burning without allowing firefighting. The staff dormitory, office, and kitchen of the farm were also burned to ashes. Later, thirteen newly built silkworm houses were demolished. Later, the police and regimental team leader came to the scene and ordered to go home. The villagers then put forward the conditions: (1) The government is not allowed to arrest the arsonist; (2) Remove Pan, the Fourth District Chief, from his post and investigate; (3) Approve the burning of Paoma Gang Silkworm Farm, the Fourth District Office, and the Qingyun Bridge Sericulture Guidance Institute; (4) In the future, if anyone buys and raises improved silkworm seeds, they should be allowed to burn their houses. The team leader thought that the matter was of great importance and had no right to accept it, so he politely explained it, but it was ineffective. The villagers poured into the city again, and all the sericulture equipment in Wenge were burned. When the villagers were setting fire in the county, the county government immediately asked the province for instructions to send troops to suppress it. At midnight, a platoon of security guards from Yuhang arrived. In order to avoid conflict, the security guards changed to Dongmen to enter the city when they arrived at Sanyanqiao, and temporarily stayed at Cisheng Temple to protect the guidance office. Around 1:00 in the middle of the night, the villagers went to Cisheng Temple again, preparing to burn the guidance office. After being dissuaded by the security guards, nothing happened. At about 4:00, the villagers began to leave in droves. This was the event on the sixth. On the 7th, the Qingshan area in the east township also had villagers gathering to plan to burn the Xihu Seed Breeding Branch. After receiving the report, the county government immediately sent the director of the Public Security Bureau to persuade them, and nothing happened. At the same time, the county government heard the news that the villagers in the west township had gathered to burn down the Paomagang Seed Breeding Farm, and sent Captain Lu to persuade them. On the same day, the villagers in the north township demolished the Fifth District Office, the residence of Dong Yizhai, the head of Hengban Town, Yu Bensheng's woodworking shop, and the cocoon shop in the area. After receiving the news, the county government asked Hu Bozheng, a member of the county executive committee, to persuade them, but it was still ineffective. On the 8th, Yun Er Township also launched a crowd to come to the city, with the slogan of destroying salt shops and rice shops and opposing the new measurement system. When they arrived at Xishu, they burned down the houses and equipment of the Linan Seed Breeding Farm. When they were about to enter the city, the county government first demolished the Sigu Bridge to prevent them from advancing. The crowd did not hesitate and still waded forward. At that time, the county chief and the company commander were both present. The county chief persuaded them with kind words, and the company commander acted as a signal to invite the village chief who led the villagers to return to his hometown, and also asked them to return to his hometown. The crowd ignored him. The security guards had no choice but to fire their guns into the sky to warn them. The villagers still waded forward, and the security guards fired their guns a second time, wounding one person with stray bullets. At that time, the villagers saw that one person had been shot and injured, and they ran away one after another, and were stopped by the commander. After the soldiers charged, they fled away. That night, the villagers in the north township sent letters to various townships, agreeing to gather again in the city to cause trouble. After learning about it, the county government immediately invited representatives from various agencies and groups, and Deng, the battalion commander of the security guards, and others to hold a meeting to discuss prevention methods, and decided: (1) The city's defense is the responsibility of the military regiment; (2) Send personnel to set out in eight directions to find out what's going on; (3) The county party department and various mass organizations will issue a public letter to the masses; (4) If the villagers gather in the city again on the 9th to cause trouble, the leaders will be arrested to maintain law and order. At noon on the 9th, according to reports, there was no significant action in Pingbiao in the west township and in the north township. Only in the eastern township, the Xihu Seed Breeding Branch had been dismantled by three or four hundred villagers from Wangjiabu and other areas in Qingshan, and Shao Qingquan, the head of the township, and his son were beaten and their residences were searched and demolished. In the southern township, the situation was still quite serious on that day. Villagers from Yaojiacun and Yinjia Village gathered three or four hundred people with gongs and drums, and went straight to Linglong, demolishing the Third District Office, and all the documents, equipment, and luggage were completely burned. The district chief had already left to avoid them, and the clerks were insulted, beaten and injured. Then they burned down all the Huatai Cocoon Shop. Then they planned to burn down the Cuisheng Seed Breeding Farm, and after the villagers and landlord Chen Quand's family in the area begged bitterly and treated them with wine, meat, and rice, they were saved, but they had to issue a guarantee that they would no longer feed foreign silkworms in the future as a condition. After the county chief learned about it, he joined forces with Battalion Commander Deng and led more than 40 security guards to suppress the situation. When they arrived at the scene, most of them had already dispersed. That night, the provincial government sent He Section Chief and other three people to the county to investigate and deal with the riots of the villagers last time. On the morning of the tenth, the county chief convened a meeting of various agencies and groups to discuss ways to quell the storm. Due to time constraints, no concrete decision has been made. The Provincial Party Department also appointed Wu Yifei to the county to investigate that day. There was no movement in the townships on that day, and the storm seemed to be calming down. As for the losses of the silkworms that were burned, it is estimated that the Xihu Seed Breeding Farm in the city and Qingshan cost more than 70,000 yuan, the Linan Seed Breeding Farm about 6,000 yuan, the Huatai Cocoon Shop about 7,000 yuan, the Hengban Cocoon Shop about 2,000 yuan, and the Yu Bensheng Woodworking Shop, Yu Shiyu, Dong Yizhai, Shi Zheng, Mao Changsheng, Lv Zhenkuan, and Shao Qingquan and other residences suffered losses due to searches and demolitions of about 5,000 yuan. The Fifth and Third District Offices were destroyed, with public and private losses of about 1,000 yuan. The loss of wine and food entertainment and other losses is about 500 yuan. In total, the material losses in this incident are about 90,000 yuan. It is said that some people seemed to have made proper plans before the riot of the villagers, and they returned to the scene to direct the incident, so it is worth noting that: (1) Most of the participants are not silkworm farmers, and there are people who have never met each other; (2) The action is rapid, the methods are consistent, and the steps are orderly; (3) The leaders have no responsible personnel from each township; (4) The on-site commanders have the same special markings. After this riot, the order in the county is not easy to stabilize for a while. The rural economy will inevitably be greatly affected. The basic organization of autonomy has also been severely hit. Local people are deeply worried and hope that the government will have effective measures to seek relief.

Wuxi

Cotton Yarn Industry in a State of Collapse 85

The Chinese cotton yarn industry has recently been unable to maintain itself due to the influx of cotton yarn and the daily decline in market prices, resulting in unbearable losses. Shanghai yarn factories have proposed a nationwide shutdown of yarn factories to all yarn factories for serious discussion, hoping to promote higher sand prices after reducing shipments. Zhang Zeming, chairman of the National Federation of Yarn Factories, came to Wuxi from Shanghai the day before yesterday to jointly consult with the leaders of Wuxi's sand factories and put forward two claims: (1) The daily decline in yarn prices makes it difficult to support this. The factories in Shanghai plan to tend towards a divided strategy and reduce production. , Increase prices invisibly. (2) Following the precedent of the silk factory industry, on the one hand, reduce work, and on the other hand, request the government to provide funds for relief. However, the factories in the Wuxi area believe that the situation is different, the impact is small, and although yarn prices have fallen, the cost of cotton is also cheaper, so they can barely support it. If the implementation reduces work, then the livelihood of workers will inevitably be affected, so it is decided to maintain the status quo temporarily.

Overseas Chinese from Mexico Arrive in Shanghai Yesterday 87

Due to the Anti-Chinese Impact in Mexico, a Total of Over 140 People

Scheduled to Go to Hong Kong Today to Return to Their Hometown and Petition the Capital, Date Not Yet Set

Far East News Agency: Overseas Chinese from Mexico were affected by the anti-Chinese sentiment of the local government and people. They cannot stand in the local country, and a part of them, more than 140 people, are on their way back to China on the Monroe President, a ship of the US Dale Company. The ship docked at the Dale Pier in Pudong at 8 am yesterday, and the Overseas Chinese Federation sent Peng Can Guang to take care of it.

The Return 88

According to Mr. Peng Canguang, general secretary of the Global Overseas Chinese Federation, there are about 20,000 overseas Chinese in Mexico. Most of them are businessmen and laborers. This time, Mexico suddenly expelled Chinese. Among them, those who are doing business have declared bankruptcy due to the anti-Chinese sentiment. Those who were laborers were suddenly unemployed, so they could not stand their ground. They all went to the United States. The United States and Mexico are adjacent to each other. The US government said that there are too many unemployed workers in the country, so it cannot accommodate so many unemployed Chinese, so it sent them back to China. The overseas Chinese planned to take the Japanese Queen of the Changxing Company back to China, but because they could not afford the fare, they changed to the American Dale Company's Monroe President to Shanghai. As for all the ship fares and food expenses, the US authorities will request our government to return them, which is the situation of this return to China.

Reason for Anti-Chinese Sentiment 89

Mr. Peng said again that the biggest reason for the anti-Chinese sentiment in Mexico this time is that there are economic recession in the international community, and the economic panic in various countries is no less than that in our country. Mexico is also forced by the recession, and the number of unemployed people in the country is increasing. Our overseas Chinese in Mexico are very developed in business, and at the same time, the labor community also occupies a very important position. Therefore, the people of that country, in order to make a living, launched an anti-Chinese movement regardless of the diplomatic relations between the two countries. Our ambassador to Mexico, Feng Chongzhi, had negotiated with the government of that country, but the government of that country not only did not stop it, but secretly directed it. This shows one aspect of the reason for the anti-Chinese sentiment in Mexico.

Petitioning the Capital 90

Most of the more than 100 people who arrived in Shanghai yesterday are from Zhongshan County, Guangdong Province. Therefore, when the ship docked, except for a few people who disembarked to visit relatives and friends, the rest did not leave the ship. They plan to take the original ship to Hong Kong today and return to their hometown. As for the representatives of the capital petition, it is said that they will be recommended on the ship. After arriving in Hong Kong, they will decide on the date of petitioning the capital. It is said that the Overseas Chinese Federation wanted to hold a welcome meeting yesterday, but it was cancelled because these overseas Chinese were scheduled to take the original ship to Hong Kong today to return to their hometown, and there was not enough time.

British Naval Expert Gluckman Discusses China's Urgent Need for a Navy 92

Says Airplanes Alone

Cannot Stop Enemy Ships

The Ta Mei Evening News reports that Rear Admiral Gluckman, a British naval expert, has been assisting the Ministry of the Navy in training naval personnel in China for two full years. Yesterday (the 10th), at a luncheon meeting of the United Youth Association, he gave a brief speech on the Chinese Navy, saying that if the Chinese Navy had won in the Sino-Japanese War, the history of the Far East would certainly be very different from what it is today. At that time, the morale of the Chinese Navy was very high, but it lacked ammunition, because the naval funds were diverted by Empress Dowager Cixi to build the Summer Palace. He also said that many people here mistakenly regard the foreign cruisers currently docked in the Huangpu River as instruments of war, but they are not. These warships can only be used for police purposes. If you want to have an elite navy, you must spend a lot of money, which is one of the biggest difficulties today. The purpose of his coming to China is to train naval personnel so that they know newer methods. It takes six years to train an officer and four years to get a good soldier, but warships can be built in two years. One more thing must be solemnly declared: their trip to China was not ordered by the British government, but only invited those who volunteered to take the job. If there were no volunteers, the British government would not send anyone. However, they often regard this trip as a pleasure because they receive such generous treatment. He also said that the navy is urgently needed by China today, but apart from the Yat Sen and the 3,000-ton light cruiser Ning Hai, there is not a single new-style warship. Later, Colonel Thomas, commander of the Shanghai Municipal Council Volunteer Corps, said that if China wants to survive in the world, it must have a navy. The current cry for 1,000 airplanes is a foolish strategy. Airplanes are only one type of weapon. If you only have airplanes but cannot prevent the enemy from sending more and stronger airplanes into the country, what's the use?

Election Rules Rules for the Shanghai Concession Chinese Ratepayers Association's Election of Representatives (Directors and Committee Members) to Attend the Shanghai Municipal Council: Article 1: All representatives (directors and committee members) of the Public Concession Chinese Ratepayers Association attending the Shanghai Municipal Council shall be elected by the Delegates' Congress of this Association. Article 2: Anyone who has resided in the Public Concession for more than five years and has one of the following qualifications shall have the right to be elected as the above-mentioned representative: (A) Paying property tax of more than fifty taels per year; (B) Paying more than one thousand two hundred taels of rent per year and paying taxes. Article 3: The Delegates' Congress of this Association must have a quorum of more than half of the representatives present in order to hold the election of the above-mentioned representatives. Article 4: A candidate must receive more than half of the votes of those present in order to be elected as the above-mentioned representative. Article 5: If the number of elected candidates is insufficient, supplementary elections shall be held for the unelected candidates with the most votes, in accordance with the number of vacancies, until the full number is elected. Article 6: The election of the above-mentioned representatives shall use the double-signature cumulative voting method. Article 7: Matters to be noted by the electors: (1) Must be present in person to vote; (2) Must use the ballot issued by this Association; (3) Must clearly write the name of the candidate; (4) Must clearly write the name of the elector. Article 8: These rules shall be implemented upon approval by the Delegates' Congress of this Association.

The matter is of great importance. In addition to sending separate letters, we hereby respectfully request that you take note and attend the meeting on time.

Aviation to Save the Nation Movement 95

Abolishing Taels and Changing to Yuan, Foreign Merchants and Various Industries are Gradually Implementing It 96

The Money Industry Association Has Agreed to Allow Heng-Character Firms to Accommodate

After all industries were ordered by the Ministry of Finance to implement the abolition of taels and the change to yuan on the 6th of this month, all silver transactions are calculated in silver yuan. Foreign merchant banks have also partially implemented it. As for the request of Heng-character money shops for the Money Industry Association to issue public orders for exchange and accommodation, a settlement has been reached. The details are as follows:

Lin Kanghou Talks to a Reporter from the New Voice Society Yesterday, a reporter met with Mr. Lin Kanghou, Secretary-General of the Bankers Association. According to him, foreign merchant banks have partially implemented the abolition of taels and the change to yuan. Since the 6th, the silver receipts and payments of Chinese merchant banks and money shops have been calculated in silver yuan according to the statutory price of 715. Since the 10th, all foreign exchange transactions have been converted from taels to yuan, and the market has been opened. Silver deposit accounts have been suspended, and silver transaction accounts have been transferred. This is the implementation of the abolition of taels. As for the silver of foreign merchant businesses, although the status quo is temporarily maintained, it will also be converted into silver yuan in the shortest possible time. Therefore, there is no problem with the abolition of taels and the change to yuan by foreign merchant businesses.

Qin Xiqing Talks Yesterday, the reporter also met with Mr. Qin Xiqing, Secretary-General of the Money Industry Association. According to him, the association has resolved that the handling of silver and foreign exchange receipts and payments on the same day by the Heng-character money shop, which is an agent of the Northern City Heng-character money shop, should be handled by the Heng-character money shop itself. Since the request for accommodation has been made, accommodation should be given. When members receive tickets from the Heng-character counterparts in the Northern City, they should bring back the receipt issued by the shop, proving the number of tickets and the amount of silver, and the balance should be cleared by the public order that night. The remaining balance should be cleared at 5:00 p.m. every day. According to the Yuan-character shops, there are funds deposited in the association, but the Heng-character shops do not have funds deposited in the association, so they must be cleared before 5:00 p.m. every day.

Lu Xuepu, the New Director of the Central Mint, Will Take Office Today 97

Guo Chengen, Director of the Central Mint, submitted his resignation to the Ministry of Finance, but it was repeatedly rejected by Minister Song. Now, Lu Xuepu, Chairman of the Shanghai Jiaotong Bank, has been appointed as his successor. After being appointed, Mr. Lu will go to the factory today to take office.

The National Government Cables Kong Xiangxi to Take Office 98

Mr. Kong Releases a Statement

Mr. Kong Xiangxi once expressed his refusal to take the post of Governor of the Central Bank offered by the National Government. On the 7th of this month, he even cabled the National Government to request the revocation of the order. Yesterday, Mr. Kong received a reply cable from the Civil Service Office of the National Government, urging him to take office immediately. It is heard that Mr. Kong will no longer firmly decline. The original cable is recorded as follows: President Kong Yongzhi Jian, I have received the Chairman's instructions and am aware of your cable. The Central Bank's business is important. I rely on your great reputation and talent to continue the scale and take on this great task. I hope you will suppress your humility and take office immediately to live up to the expectations. The request to revoke the order should not be discussed, etc. In particular, Wei Huai, Chief of Civil Servants of the National Government, pays his respects.

This morning, Mr. Kong Xiangxi told a reporter from the Central News Agency that since Minister Song resigned from the post of Governor of the Central Bank due to his busy schedule, the Central Government immediately ordered him to take over. At that time, he cabled his resignation. Since returning from overseas, he has naturally worked hard in this time of national crisis, but he does not need to bear any title. During the period of national crisis, the government organization should not be changed too much. Minister Song has served as Governor of the Bank for a long time, and the Bank was founded by Mr. Song. Therefore, it is better for Mr. Song to resume his post in order to have a skilled person. However, since he resigned, he has not received a formal cable order from the Central Government, so he does not want to make any expression. Mr. Kong continued to talk about the great importance of the World Economic Preparatory Meeting held in the United States. Our country should fully prepare to send someone familiar with our country's economic situation to attend for reference. It is rumored that Minister Song will be sent to participate. He has gained a slight understanding of the current economic situation in various countries during this trip to Europe and the United States, and is willing to contribute it to the government for reference.

Two Concession Municipal Councils Collect Silver Yuan for Property Tax Starting from April 99

Both Electricity and Telephone Companies Charge According to 715

Taxpayers' Association Hopes Citizens Will Pay According to the Fixed Rate

The Guowen News Agency reports that since the Ministry of Finance explicitly ordered the implementation of the abolition of taels and the change to yuan, and the calculation based on the 715 silver standard starting from the 6th of this month, the silver and money industries, various industries, and foreign merchant banks in this city have all followed suit. The Chinese Ratepayers' Association of the Public Concession in this city sent a special letter to the Shanghai Municipal Council the day before yesterday, hoping that the council would also convert the property tax collection into silver yuan at the legal price of 7 qian 1 fen and 5 li, and hoped that public utilities such as electricity, telephone, and tap water would also change to collecting silver yuan in the same way. A reporter from the Guowen News Agency visited the Shanghai Municipal Council, the Electricity Company, and the Telephone Company yesterday to inquire, and they all said that they would follow suit starting from this month. The Chinese Taxpayers' Association issued a statement yesterday, hoping that citizens would implement the 715 conversion payment uniformly. The details are recorded as follows:

Shanghai Municipal Council to Follow Suit 100

Yesterday, a reporter visited the Shanghai Municipal Council of the Public Concession and inquired about the council's opinion on the letter from the Chinese Ratepayers' Association requesting that the property tax collection be changed to the 75 silver price. According to the council's spokesperson, the council has always been sympathetic to the Chinese government's efforts to unify the currency system and has tried its best to assist within the possible scope. Now that the Chinese government has explicitly ordered the implementation of the abolition of taels and the change to yuan, and the currency system is calculated at the legal silver price of 715, the council has decided that starting from this month (April), all citizens within the concession who pay property tax may pay according to the 715 calculation and conversion. The Shanghai Municipal Council will collect them uniformly, etc.

Electricity and Telephone Implemented 101

Then, the reporter visited the Electricity Company's chief accountant, who said that the Electricity Company had already followed suit since the Chinese government began implementing the abolition of taels and the change to yuan and set the legal silver price of 715, starting from last Saturday (the 9th). In the future, electricity users who come to the company to pay fees can all be converted at the 715 silver price, he said. In addition, according to the secretary and district manager of the Telephone Company, who spoke to a reporter from the Guowen News Agency, the Telephone Company will of course take the same action as the Shanghai Municipal Council, etc. After the 715 silver price was set, the company has been charging according to this price for several days. For example, if you (referring to the reporter) go to the company's collection office today and pay at the 715 silver price, there will be no complications, he said.

French Shanghai Municipal Council Implemented 102

The French Concession Municipal Council replied to the First Special District Citizens' Union, saying that the council's tax office has been ordered by the council that starting from April 1, all taxes collected will be calculated at the 715 legal price, etc.

Statement of the Taxpayers' Association 103

According to the responsible spokesperson of the Chinese Taxpayers' Association, who spoke to a reporter from the Guowen News Agency, the association follows national laws and regulations and complies with the Ministry of Finance's explicit order to abolish taels and change to yuan with a 715 conversion silver price, and has written to the Shanghai Municipal Council to request that the tax collection and the charging of public utilities should also be handled in accordance with the regulations. Therefore, it is hoped that citizens will uniformly handle the payment of fees according to this method starting from this month, on the one hand, to implement the order, so as not to violate national laws and regulations, and on the other hand, if the Shanghai Municipal Council's tax collection staff refuse to accept the 715 silver price, they can report the situation to the association so that it can negotiate on their behalf. It is hoped that all citizens will see this statement and implement it uniformly. The association will not issue another notice, etc.

Military Instructor of Datong University Arrested 104

By Order of the Military Supervision Department to Take Office

Arrested by Order of the Military Supervision Department

The Pacific Society reports that since the establishment of military training at Datong University in Shanghai, military training specialists have been hired every semester. At the beginning of this semester (that is, in February of the Gregorian calendar), a person named Dai Chengzhi suddenly went to the school with an order from the Military Supervision and Training Department and asked to see Principal Wang Boqun. Wang was out on official business, so Vice-Principal Ou Yuanhuai received him. He thought that since Dai had come to the school to take office by order of the Military Supervision Department, there was no reason to refuse him. He immediately obeyed the order and asked him to come to the school to take office. Unexpectedly, this was a fraudulent situation. Dai Chengzhi was suddenly arrested by the Garrison Command yesterday. A reporter from the Pacific Society found this matter to be quite bizarre, so he went to the Garrison Department to interview. The details obtained are recorded below:

Fraudulent Process 105

Dai Chengzhi, a native of Wuxi, 22 years old, wearing a Western suit and leather shoes, with an elegant demeanor, went to Datong University in Shanghai in early February of the Gregorian calendar with an order from the Military Supervision Department and asked to see Principal Wang Boqun. Wang was out on official business, so Vice-Principal Ou Yuanhuai received him. Ou thought that since Dai had come here by order of the Military Supervision Department to take on military training, he should be treated favorably. He approved a monthly salary of 80 yuan. Not long after Dai took on the job of military training, he applied to the school authorities, saying that he had now received an order from the Military Supervision Department to concurrently serve as a military instructor at Datong University in addition to Datong University. However, the certificate from the Wuxi Private Middle School that he is currently using is no longer applicable and needs to be changed in Beijing to conform to reality, and requested leave in advance and the salary for the first month. The school authorities said that it was difficult to fully pay in advance because classes had not yet started, so they gave Dai 20 yuan. A few days later, Dai arrived wearing the military instructor badge of Datong University. The school authorities had no doubts. After the school started, Dai was asked to implement training. Unexpectedly, around March 20, Dai asked the school authorities for leave to return to his hometown to complete his marriage. The school also granted him 60 yuan in salary. After a few days, Dai returned to school and continued to work as usual.

Garrison Ordered 106

The Longhua Garrison Command received a secret order from the Military Training Department a few days ago, stating that a person named Dai Chengzhi had fraudulently used an order from the department to go to Datong University and fraudulently take away his salary. The matter concerned military affairs and was ordered to be secretly arrested and sent to Beijing for interrogation. No one should be allowed to escape, etc. Upon receiving the order, the Garrison Department immediately ordered Adjutant Zheng Letian to secretly go to the school to arrest him and bring him to justice for interrogation.

Process of Arrest 107

Adjutant Zheng Letian of the Garrison Department received a secret order from his superiors and immediately took a car to the school to arrest him. However, Dai had not returned from completing his marriage, so he was unable to arrest him. Until yesterday, Dai returned to school and was in class directing training when Zheng suddenly showed him the secret order of the Training Supervision Department, stating that he knew. Dai initially argued strongly, saying that since the Supervision Department had sent his brother here, how could he be arrested by order of the Supervision Department again? He implied that he could not obey the order. However, since the Garrison Department had received a formal order, it had to obey the order to arrest him. Dai knew that there was no way to recover, so he and Zheng took a car to the Garrison Department for temporary detention.

Dai's Statement 108

When a reporter from the Pacific Society met with Dai, he asked him how he dared to commit such a great impropriety. Dai sighed and said to the reporter, "At this time of economic recession and overstaffing, it is really difficult to find a bite to eat by any means. Rather than falling into the underworld, it is better to take a chance, or perhaps get lucky. Now that I have been caught, I did not intend to do this, but I was really forced by life." After speaking, he sighed for a long time.

To Be Sent to Beijing This Morning 109

After the Garrison Department arrested Dai, it slightly interrogated him at the Military Law Department because the matter concerned the arrest of a person designated by his superiors. A platoon of military police was sent to Beijing this morning to escort him and bring him to justice for interrogation.

Repercussions of the French Concession Police Suppressing Night Work 110

Jiu Yi Da Ming Fined Successively

Qiu Zhi Socks Factory Also Intervened

The Shanghai Knitwear Industry Guild presented a petition to the Municipal Government yesterday, stating, "Presenting this petition regarding the French Concession police obstructing work and extorting fines, endangering the entire industry and potentially violating French rights, earnestly requesting serious negotiations to halt these actions." According to a letter from a member, the Qiu Zhi Knitwear Factory, "We respectfully inform you that our factory is located at the intersection of Fulu Li Road and Yapei Road in Guangyu Li, within the factory zone designated by the French Concession authorities. We have been operating day and night for years, and this is not a new occurrence. Unexpectedly, at 2:00 AM on the 7th of this month, while our factory was operating, a Western police officer No. 29 from the French Concession, accompanied by a Chinese police officer, abruptly broke down the factory door, invaded the workshop, and forcefully demanded an immediate work stoppage. At 8:00 AM the next morning, Chinese police officer No. 330 was dispatched to the factory to extort a fine of five silver dollars, issuing a standard French Concession police fine receipt. Surprisingly, on the 9th, the same Chinese police officer was dispatched to the factory again to extort another fine. We believe that knitwear factories are legitimate businesses, and day and night work is not prohibited by law, especially within the factory zone. Operating overnight is not unique to our factory, nor is it unique to Chinese-owned factories. We do not know what police regulations were violated by this fine. Does the French Concession police ordinance explicitly restrict factories within the factory zone from operating at night? Is this regulation applied equally to Chinese and foreign factories? The Western police officer, as a public official, invaded a taxpayer's factory late at night and forced a work stoppage without any basis. If it is claimed that working late at night disturbs people's sleep, then the Lujiawan Power Plant, located nearby, also operates overnight and is in the same factory zone, and its noise is dozens or even hundreds of times louder than our factory. This time, our factory has been unjustly oppressed, ultimately leading to a factory shutdown, which has a minor impact. Other Chinese national factories may also be forced to shut down one by one. Therefore, we must request your esteemed association to petition the government and various public organizations to negotiate firmly with the French Concession authorities to uphold justice." Investigations revealed that there is no explicit order from our government prohibiting night work, nor is there such a regulation in the so-called Concession police ordinance. Recently, the French Concession authorities have frequently arbitrarily punished factories operating late at night within the Concession. What is the basis for this? Moreover, if this punishment is indeed based on the administrative regulations of the Concession, then, according to the agreement on the establishment of a Chinese court within the Shanghai French Concession, the police should bring a lawsuit to the court for trial. The fact that the police dispatched officers to extort fines and issue fine receipts clearly violates the agreement and jeopardizes our national legal rights. Moreover, the Qiu Zhi Factory is located within the designated factory zone. If night work is not allowed within the factory zone, then why have factory and residential zones been designated? Furthermore, Qiu Zhi Factory is not the only factory operating at night, nor is it the only industry doing so. It is difficult to consider the police's arbitrary obstruction of work and extortion of fines as appropriate. Our association has received reports from members such as Jiu Yi Da..., the situation is similar to the previous letter. We respectfully request your esteemed bureau to forward this to the French Concession authorities for legal advocacy, serious negotiations, and to halt their unreasonable interference and extortion of fines, in order to protect sovereignty and maintain the real economy. We eagerly await this.
