Free Talk

Dissent on "Killing the Wrong Person" 188

— He Jia Gan

After reading Mr. Cao Juren's article "Killing the Wrong Person," I felt very happy, but thinking back, I felt that some of it was still inevitable talk of anger, so I wanted to raise a few objections:

After the Xinhai Revolution, Yuan Shikai massively killed party members. From Yuan Shikai's perspective, he did not kill the wrong person at all, because he was a fake revolutionary and a counter-revolutionary.

What was wrong was that the revolutionaries were deceived, thinking that he was really a somersault, changing from a Beiyang minister to a revolutionary, so they introduced him as a comrade, shed everyone's blood, and floated him to the presidential throne. By the Second Revolution, on the surface, it seemed that he was another somersault, changing from a "public servant of the people" to a blood-sucking demon, but in fact, it was not. He was just showing his true colors again.

So, kill, kill, kill. In Beijing, even the hotels and inns were full of detectives; there was also the "Military and Political Enforcement Office," where only suspected youths were seen being sent in, but they were never seen walking out alive; also, in the "Government Gazette," there were advertisements every day for party members leaving the party, saying that they had been pulled in by friends before, mistakenly joined the party, now they knew their mistakes, and would leave from now on, to wash their minds and become good people.

Soon it proved that Yuan Shikai did not kill the wrong people, he wanted to be emperor.

This matter has been twenty years in the blink of an eye. The young people in their twenties now were still sucking milk then. Time is so fast.

But, Yuan Shikai wanted to be emperor himself, so why did he leave his real enemy, the old emperor? There is no need for much discussion. Just look at the current warlord melee to know. They fight to the death, as if they are irreconcilable, but in the end, as long as one "steps down," they will be polite to each other. However, for revolutionaries, even if they have not fought, they will never let one go. They know very well.

So I think that the Chinese revolution has become like this, not because they "killed the wrong person," but because we saw the wrong person.

Finally, I also have a little objection to the proposal of "killing more people over middle age," but because I am already "over middle age," to avoid suspicion, I will just look at the ground.

Fishing Platform and West Platform

— Cao Juren

Yan Ziling's Fishing Platform on the Fuchun River has recently had a stroke of luck, favored by modern women; many Shanghai celebrities have made a special trip to Qililong to visit it. The cliff is very high, the mountain road is very narrow, climbing from the foot of the mountain to the top is covered in sweat; a few broken houses, a few broken steles, there is nothing good to see, so they return in disappointment, thinking "there is no reason." For the sake of "elegance," they can't say the suffering: I have been to the place where Mr. Fan Wenzheng has been, which is worth it, so there is a poem as proof.

People who visit the fishing platform are mostly good at research: how did Mr. Yan fish on such a high platform back then? Everyone studies how long the fishing rod is, how long the fishing line is, maybe they discuss how many fish can be caught every day. They treat Mr. Yan as a humorous fisherman and think of many interesting fishing methods for him. But Fan Hua doesn't do good, and the Book of the Later Han says: "There is a man, wearing a sheepskin coat, fishing in the marsh." Too little poetry! Too little poetry!

Connected to the fishing platform, there is another dangerous cliff. Fabricated archaeologists say it is Jiang Taigong's Fishing Platform: nine out of ten passers-by in Qililong are Jiang Taigong's party, supporting this saying. They say: "The perch on the Xunyang River is the seed of Qililong; one day, Jiang Taigong caught a perch, shook it hard, broke free of the hook, and flew to the Xunyang River." That perch was probably a pregnant woman. As far as I know, it was the West Platform where Xie Gaoyu beat the zhu (ancient stringed instrument) and wept in pain at the end of the Southern Song Dynasty, with the Record of the Weeping on the West Platform recording this painful event of national demise.

Xie Gaoyu naturally cannot win the favor of Shanghai celebrities; what does it matter if the country is destroyed, they can still enjoy themselves happily, to come to such a scenic place to beat the zhu and weep in pain is the number one fool in the world. So the Southern Song Dynasty is only six or seven hundred years away from now and has long disappeared from people's memories; while the elegant ancestor two thousand years ago is remembered by people thousands of years later and has recently had a stroke of luck. It can be seen that it is best for ancient people to be sensible and know how to have fun. People in the Southern Dynasty were already praising the scenery of Fuchun endlessly. In Wu Jun's Letter to Song Yuansi, "The wind and smoke are all gone, the sky and mountains share the same color, drifting with the current, freely east and west, from Fuyang to Tonglu, more than a hundred miles, the strange mountains and beautiful waters are unique in the world." This is such a desirable place. Light rain, heavy fog, new moon, dawn, the taste of this, the man wearing a sheepskin coat fishing in the marsh, he understands and enjoys it very much! Unfortunately, we were not born at the right time, and when we should be climbing the West Platform to beat the zhu and weep in pain, we are still not allowed to "drift with the current, freely east and west"!

Dance

— Luo Hong

The white electric light went out lazily. Tempting dim light leaked from the modern ceiling. This light was so dazing and mesmerizing. Following this light spread in the space was the music of the popular Fox-trot dance. So one by one, flattering and proud men used the most fashionable posture in the social scene and walked towards those dancers. Two by two, young men and women rotated on the glittering floor, with light smiles floating on their faces.

He was sitting. His eyes jumped among these rotating people. Watching and listening, he pressed his breath slowly, because he wanted to suppress his heartbeat. He remembered the first time he went to the dance hall with Lao Huang, he was also so panicked by the heartbeat. He said that such carnal temptation was disgusting, and Lao Huang laughed at him for being too pedantic. Good-hearted friends happily forced him to learn, and he, who was very smart in reading, was also very smart in this regard. Friends taught him a few times, and he was already dancing pretty well. Tonight, Lao Huang didn't know where he got the idea and pulled him along again. He was so panicked again. Waves of fragrance, one by one, half-naked bodies, twisting in various poses, made his every nerve tremble slightly. He smiled bitterly. He looked at Lao Huang hugging a short dancer, skillfully moving his steps with the rhythm of the music. Lao Huang's face was floating with a greedy smile, and most of the faces of other men also had this greedy smile. He felt a kind of embarrassing disgust, but the music stopped at this time.

Lao Huang took a sip of tea and looked at him with a proud eye. "Come on, the one in the red dress just danced very well."

He smiled bitterly.

"Are you going to be pedantic again? What's the matter?" Lao Huang said, smiling triumphantly. He wanted to say something more, but was stopped by the music. Lao Huang went with the music again. The light shed from the ceiling changed from light green to light purple.

The air became more and more fragrant, and also mixed with the strong taste of champagne. The intoxication of wine, the intoxication of flesh, smeared those greedy faces with a layer of blush. But his emotions slowly calmed down. When the music sounded again, he also walked to a dancer like others. She was wearing long hair that had been ironed by a top barber, and a thin gauze dress covered her well-proportioned body. He moved his steps subconsciously, and his heart jumped subconsciously again. Now he saw clearly the faces that often pretended to be delicate, with a layer of dim wrinkles faintly hidden under the powder, and the bewildered eyes contained a dim bitter smile. The wheels of the city devoured her into this appearance.

"Ah, behind the joy, such a bitter smile flashes?" he said in his heart. Following the music that slowly quieted down, he lowered his head and returned to his original seat.

Red light leaked from the ceiling again.

Philosophy of Life

— Bo Fu

(1)

Our life is like sitting in Columbus's ship. When we set out, we don't know where we are going. When we arrive, we don't know where we are. When we come back, we don't know where we have been.

(2)

If you meet someone who is greater than you, you can conclude that he is greater than you in two ways. That is, he is better at telling lies, and he is a more utter bastard!

(3)

All lovers are bound to be theorists, because what they say is rarely put into practice.

(4)

When you meet a stranger, don't ask who he is, what you should ask is whose man he is!

Flower Gambling

— Li

"Ban Gua Cai in Fang Maolin, Taiping Shengshi Xu Yuangui, Fengchun Deshi Zhu Guangming, Huoguan Liancheng Lin Genyu..." Not to mention the bumpkins in other places, even five or six-year-old street urchins can recite the Flower Gambling rhymes by heart. "What a pity, a good Zhang Huoguan, hesitant and indecisive, sadly gave up!"

"Still need to talk about it? Last night I dreamed of a house on fire, so accurate. For some reason, he went to bet on Li Mingzhu. Why strike the clams when you can strike the turkey? Where did that come from?" In eight out of ten villages, there were gatherings of men and women. In the morning, they talked about dreams, at noon they waited for news, in the afternoon they discussed Flower Gambling lore, and in the evening men and women mingled and went to deserted temples and graveyards to pray for dreams. Some even stole from the bodhisattvas, picked up corpses, and made gambling wagers by weighing them, steaming them, and other unspeakable things.

People are seven parts ghost-like, talking ghost stories endlessly, filled with the idea of getting rich quick. Everyone is a character from the Legend of the Obsessed with Wealth, where is there any humanity left? Strange news emerges one after another. Obsessed with wealth, cutting off their own son's head, chopping off their own daughter's arm to bet on Flower Gambling has become a commonly told tale.

The gambling opens every day, paying out thirty times the stake. It's simple, and the profits are high, no wonder it's sweeping the countryside, old and young enthusiastically participate. Inoue Koubai, a Japanese who is known as a "China expert," once used wine, mahjong, and opium as symbols of China, and wrote a thick book, grandiosely telling the Japanese people. This treasure came to China, gambled heavily, patronized prostitutes, exclusively fraternized with hooligans, and colluded with thugs, messing around in the underworld for a while, and then thought that China was such a country. At first, when I saw that book, I was really angry. But what's the use of being angry? Not only are the petty citizens in the city decadent and unbearable, but now even the farmers in the countryside have learned to speculate and take advantage of opportunities. Everyone has a heart of adventure and luck. The title of the country of wine, mahjong, and opium has become truly deserved. A nation that has decayed to this point, where is there any hope of revival!

Full-Length Novel

The Crossroads of Era and Love

— Zhang Ziping

"In case I participate in a demonstration parade this afternoon and am caught by the running dogs of imperialism, then I will have absolutely no experience with the opposite sex."

Such a self-deprecating thought further prompted his expression to her. He felt hot all over. He hugged her neck at this moment.

"Mr. Lin!..."

She just smiled foolishly. Her body seemed to be softening. When he saw her pursing her lips to express herself to him, he hugged her tightly like a hungry eagle catching a small sparrow.

Afterward, he also felt that kissing the opposite sex was not so tasty. He seemed to smell the fishy smell of her saliva. He thought, could it be that she ate canned sardines this morning.

Thirty-Three

When he arrived at Tang Yaoxing's residence, it was a quarter past twelve. He saw only a young man with a peaked cap on his head, a blue cloth long gown on his body, and a pale face sitting in Yaoxing's room. The whole room was cold and clear, not like a place for group meetings. Haiquan greeted the young man, but did not ask his name, and sat down on the edge of Tang Yaoxing's bed in a grand manner.

"Where did Lao Tang go?"

Haiquan asked half to the young man and half to himself.

"He will be back in a moment."

The young man answered him very readily.

Sure enough, Tang Yaoxing came back after a moment. As soon as he saw Haiquan, he questioned Haiquan in a very imposing manner.

"Why don't you obey the rules?"

"Didn't I come?"

Haiquan replied with a smiling face. At first, he only thought that Yaoxing was joking with him, but looking at Yaoxing's pale face with a stern look, which had not loosened at all, he restrained his smile, but held a little resentment in his heart.

"I told you to come here at twelve o'clock, why didn't you keep the time?"

Guangdong Merchants Fiercely Dump About 3,000 Bars

The Spot Price Briefly Rises to 1,100 Yuan

A Deluge of Bad News Causes Prices to Break Below 90 Yuan Again After Closing

The gold market experienced a significant downturn yesterday, mainly due to reports that U.S. Secretary of State Hull had proposed three ways to increase silver prices, causing widespread anxiety. Although London spot prices rose nearly 1.25 pence and forward prices rose 1.875 pence, New York silver prices surged 6.25 cents, with forward prices rising even more sharply, soaring over 8 cents. Private telegraphic transfers rose to 8.125, and American cotton also increased by four points, causing the gross price to drop to 934 yuan, before rising to 78 yuan. The market opened at 1,095.8 yuan in the morning, and the exchange rate also opened strong, causing prices to fall. After the Shanghai and Hong Kong Banking Corporation (HSBC) announced its rates, with both the British and American exchange rates increasing by only 1.25 pence, the exchange market tightened slightly, and prices rose slightly. However, the afternoon session saw a small drop. The market opened steadily in the afternoon, but then banks' appetite improved, and the spot price rose, stabilizing sentiment and briefly surging to 1,100 yuan. However, with Bombay initially rising nine annas, followed by another three annas, and news of a silver price conference circulating from foreign sources, the exchange rate remained strong, and the gold market continued to decline, closing at 1,091.3 yuan. After the market closed, news of further actions favorable to silver prices in the United States emerged, causing prices to break below the 90 yuan level, with the downward trend remaining strong. Throughout the day, the market situation was difficult to support. Guangdong merchants fiercely sold approximately 3,000 bars (handled by the Tuota firm). Three Announcements from the Gold Exchange 190

Regulations Regarding Trading Hours

Advance Swap Transactions

Western Holiday Closure for Three Days

Regarding the letter from our exchange's Brokers Association, proposing to change the date for starting term swap transactions to 3:00 PM on the 15th of each month. If that date falls on a Wednesday, Saturday, or Sunday, it will be moved to 10:00 AM, and if it's a holiday, it will be moved to the previous day. However, no new monthly term trading is allowed on the swap date; all new monthly term trading will commence on the following day, etc. Since this matter has been deemed feasible by the Brokers Association, it is approved to be implemented on a trial basis starting this month. Strict adherence to the regulations is essential. This is hereby announced.

The matters to be handled are listed below:

(1) The bell will ring at 3:00 PM (10:00 AM on Wednesdays, Saturdays, and Sundays) to start swap transactions.

(2) The board will be hung on the upper row of the west side (upper row of the east side on Wednesdays, Saturdays, and Sundays).

(3) The swap buyer will post a red "buy" or "sell" card, and the seller will post a "buy" or "sell" card.

(4) Black cards will be used for price quotations (yuan and jiao).

(5) If there is a fluctuation of 0.5 jiao or more, the price will continue to be posted until 4:30 PM.

(6) If there is a difference of 0.4 jiao in the daily account, it will be collected.

(7) Only term swap accounts will be collected on that day; new monthly term accounts will not be collected.

(8) Only new monthly term prices will be posted on the following day.

This month, the May 15th swap falls on a holiday, so the swap will start early on the 13th at 3:00 PM after the bell rings, but only swap transactions are allowed. New trading for the June contract will commence on the 18th of this month. This is hereby announced.

The banks will be closed for holidays on the 14th, 15th, and 17th of this month, and our exchange will also be closed for three days. This is hereby announced.

Foreign Exchange: Tightening and Loosening Intermittently 191

| Eventually, All Hardened |

According to foreign news, London spot cable rose 1.25 pence, forward cable rose 1.875 pence, British to American exchange rate was down 0.375, and American to British exchange rate was unchanged. The opening bid for near-term British exchange was 1 shilling, 2 pence, 3.125 (or 3.75) farthings, about 1.25 farthings stronger than the previous close. New York silver prices rose 6.25 cents, and forward silver prices on the precious metals exchange rose by 8.6%. Private telegraphic transfers rose by 8.125, and American cotton also rose by four points. The opening bid for near-term American exchange was 20.5 yuan, 1.875 stronger than the previous close. The market opened strong, but banks were still buying. HSBC's published rates showed that both British and American exchange rates rose by 1.25 pence. Commentary

Should Settle the Accounts Before Leaving 209

— Niu

Laughable Words of Zhang Xueliang Before Leaving

Mr. Zhang Xueliang boarded a ship to go abroad the night before last. Many important figures from the National Government saw him off. We should also board the ship to see him off. The National Government officials' farewell represents the government's intention, while our farewell represents the general public's sentiment.

Zhang Xueliang was a hereditary king of the Northeast. Under the "non-resistance policy," he gratuitously surrendered the four northeastern provinces. Now, he is comfortably going to Italy. It is fortunate that he did not also surrender Tianjin and Beiping before leaving, which shows his good sense. However, we truly admire Mr. Zhang's spirit of "what's mine is yours, and what's yours is mine." Not only do we Chinese admire it, but many foreigners also admire it. I saw in a Western newspaper that a bronze statue should be cast for Mr. Zhang as a god of world peace. Therefore, I believe that Mr. Zhang will definitely receive a grand welcome from foreigners on this trip abroad.

But everyone already knows Mr. Zhang's past great achievements, and there have been many congratulatory articles about him. I won't add more superfluous words of praise. However, regarding this trip abroad, there are still two accounts that Mr. Zhang should clarify before leaving:

1. Before leaving Beiping, Zhang Xueliang, without authorization, sold the entire land and buildings of the Haibu Tianjin Hospital school site to the French Concession authorities where the medical school was located. After Haibu noticed this, he repeatedly telegraphed Zhang to stop it, but received no response from Zhang.

2. Zhang Ji telegraphed Mayor Wu on the 8th, saying that upon reading the newspaper, he learned that Zhang Xueliang was about to leave the country by ship. Although the bronze ware of the Summer Palace had been moved south, many ancient calligraphy and paintings from the garden were in Zhang Xueliang's possession. He suggested that they should be promptly retrieved and detained so that national treasures would not be lost overseas.

Regarding the two matters above, not only should Zhang Xueliang clarify them before leaving, but the government should also make Zhang clarify them before allowing him to go abroad. (1) The school site has already been forcibly occupied by the French Concession authorities, who led French soldiers and police to seize all the buildings of the school. Besides submitting separate petitions to the Supreme Military Authorities and the Executive Yuan to protest to the French, the National Government should cancel this unlawful contract of confusing jurisdictional systems and selling state-owned property to foreigners without authorization, and punish Zhang Xueliang for the crime of selling state-owned property to foreigners without authorization. If this matter is not resolved properly, it could cause a major dispute between China and France in the future, another calamity created by Mr. Zhang Xueliang, and another great achievement granted by Mr. Zhang Xueliang. (2) Regarding the Summer Palace calligraphy and paintings mentioned in the telegram, it is unknown how many books are in the Summer Palace collection. Mr. Zhang Xueliang should provide a clear statement, indicating how many items he took from the Summer Palace. If he does not clarify this, if some unscrupulous people follow Mr. Zhang's example in the future, everyone will blame Mr. Zhang, and you will have no way to defend yourself. This is something that Mr. Zhang should clarify. Furthermore, from the government's perspective, they should also make Zhang Xueliang clarify this matter before allowing him to go abroad, because these are mostly our national property, not private property. If anything is missing, the people should have the right to audit the government's accounts. Therefore, the government should not allow Zhang Xueliang to take these national treasures privately. Moreover, according to Zhang Ji's telegram, although the bronze ware has been moved south, the calligraphy and paintings are mostly in his hands. If the common people are ignorant and misunderstand, thinking that this is clearly a division of spoils—I take the hard and heavy items, and you take the soft and light items—a kind of harmonious cooperative action.

Page 16

How will the government explain this? Based on these two points alone, the government should not allow Zhang Xueliang to take the calligraphy and paintings away. Of course, with jackals and wolves in power, who cares about foxes? Zhang Xueliang's crime of humiliating the nation and losing territory has not even been investigated. Why should we bother him with mere ancient calligraphy, paintings, school land, and property? The government has a broad network of laws, treating the people and their possessions kindly, which is truly unprecedented and unparalleled in the world. However, if this is the case, everyone will emulate Mr. Zhang Xueliang: everyone gives away land, everyone takes things. Since there is a precedent to follow, everyone might as well emulate it. I ask, what kind of country will this become? I am not dissatisfied with Mr. Zhang, but I am truly sorry for the country.

What is even more laughable is that before leaving, Zhang Xueliang made a so-called statement, saying, "Although I resign and go abroad, not concerning myself with military or political affairs, as a member of the nation, I have a duty to both the country and the world. I will return home soon to fulfill my responsibilities." I ask, readers, think about it, are these words suitable for Zhang Xueliang to say? Mr. Zhang held important positions for many years and completely surrendered the four provinces of our country. Where was his duty then? Is it that one does not need to fulfill one's duty while in office, but only as a member of the nation can one fulfill one's duty? And he says he will return home soon to fulfill his responsibilities. Is it that he did not need to fulfill his duties before, but only after going abroad can he fulfill them? Ah! I understand now. Mr. Zhang's so-called duty and fulfilling his responsibilities refer to the duty of surrendering land, the duty of privately selling school property and stealing objects. Mr. Zhang's duty has been fulfilled enough; please don't bother to worry about it anymore.

Blood 210

— Hong

Opening the newspaper, one sees that social news of deaths in various ways is recorded almost every day; in fact, in the eyes of some people, it's as ordinary as the death of a dog!

"Ah! Oh no! Is someone about to be run over?"

As I was wandering at the entrance of the lane where I lived, a milkman on a bicycle collided head-on with a speeding motorcycle. Needless to say, the milk and bottles were all sacrificed. Then, a white-haired old man was thrown into my view, lying on the ground rolling around, his mouth uttering intermittent cries of pain! The bicycle stood there as if stunned, staring blankly at the old man. Soon, a crowd of onlookers gathered around.

"Hey, friend, are you still in pain?" The motorcyclist understood that in the real world, only power matters; anyway, power is justice. So he boldly continued, "Haha, what are you crying about? You should be glad I didn't break the car window; if I had, you wouldn't be able to afford to pay for it. At least ten taels of silver for a piece, you know, this glass is genuine imported stuff."

"Ya...oh...it hurts so much! Hurt..." The old man kept pressing his hand over the blood flowing from his mouth, crying out in pain.

"Hmm! You're making sense? Look, he's bleeding! You don't seem to hear his cries? Alas, you hit someone and you're still being stubborn?" Indignant, I "reprimanded" the motorcyclist, hoping that he would be more careful driving next time. But, as a result, he adopted the attitude of a so-called "gangster"!

"Sir, don't be fierce. I've been driving for many years. This kind of small thing, humph! What does it matter?" "Then why didn't you honk your horn? This is the entrance to a lane, you know?"

"Hehe, not honking the horn?" He said coldly, "What's so strange about that? My boss is a foreigner. He doesn't honk the horn even in the 'middle of the road', let alone for someone like you."

"Oh? You're really trying to rely on foreigners to justify your unreasonable behavior? You traitor! Everyone, look at how arrogant he is!"

"I'm scared to death. My teeth were knocked out, three of them, three! My clothes are torn to shreds."

"Hateful, drag him to ××!"

"Oh, no, Lu A'qiao, no, I don't agree. What's ×× all about? Maybe the old man will be fined. I say, make the motorcyclist pay some money and send him to the hospital." The crowd argued in various ways as above.

Everything is like this, no matter how big the matter is, there will always be an end. Soon, everyone dispersed, only the pile of blood was still red! But in a while, the cleaner will come and sweep it clean, and it will disappear without a trace.

Literature and Art

Spring Chill 211

—

Feng Zongyao

Peeking at the garden, I long for the flowers to bloom, the desolate east wind is too lazy to trim them, thoughts of returning home are blocked by the cloud shadows, poetic feelings rely entirely on the wine cup to open up.

Passing the New Year, accompanied by the old year, the Yellow River is blocked by ice, and the sky is covered by fog, the God of Spring is ashamed to see the idle flowers and grass, lingering in the slanting sun beside the ancient fort.

Clerk Correspondence

An Unswallowable Grievance 212

Editor:

I am a weak and ignorant woman. When I was seven years old, my father passed away, leaving my mother and me behind. Since then, life has been very difficult. Fortunately, I have my uncle to rely on. I am now twenty-three years old. When I was seventeen, I was studying at a certain middle school in Shanghai. Although my uncle was generous in providing me with tuition fees, he was very stubborn. He thought I was old enough and that Shanghai was a confusing place. He believed that a woman with some basic education could establish herself in society, so why seek further education? Therefore, I dropped out of school. Later, through my uncle's friend Mr. Zhu, I was introduced to a bookstore as a sales clerk, where I met a colleague, Mr. Wang. Mr. Wang was very knowledgeable and his character was not bad, so I often asked him for advice, and Mr. Wang taught me diligently without getting tired of it. Over time, our friendship turned into mutual understanding. Mr. Wang was not yet married and repeatedly proposed to me. I thought Mr. Wang was very sincere and I could rely on him for life. I discussed it with my mother, who also thought so, and we made a lifelong agreement, happily and passionately. My will was very weak, and love led to a physical relationship. Later, I repeatedly urged him to get married soon and start living together. Mr. Wang postponed it due to economic constraints. Who knew that as a result of the January 28th Incident, the bookstore closed and Mr. Wang and I had to separate. However, we still communicated by letter from time to time. Recently, for the past three months, Mr. Wang suddenly changed his ways, stopped writing letters, and when I wrote to him, he did not reply. After inquiring repeatedly, I learned that he had broken his previous promise and became engaged to Miss Zheng and married her on the twelfth of last month. When I heard this, my heart was like a knife. I went to argue with him, but he claimed that it was his parents' order and he could not refuse. When I went again, he avoided meeting me, leaving me with tears flowing onto my pillow. Later, my uncle found out and questioned me constantly. What face do I have to answer him? Now Mr. Wang used seductive means to lure me, causing me to lose my chastity, and finally abandoned me halfway, leaving me with a茫茫future. I am a weak woman, how can I deal with him? If I let it go like this, how can I swallow this grievance? The only way out is to commit suicide, but suicide is despicable and useless. Should I resolve it through legal means? But the verbal agreement is not documented, and it is unknown whether the crimes of breaching a marriage agreement and rape can be established. Therefore, I sincerely ask you, sir, to open a bright path and help me resolve this matter. I believe that you, sir, are dedicated to society and will definitely grant me guidance. Respectfully requesting your peace, Lu Kunzhen respectfully writes.

Editor's Note: After reading Miss Lu's letter, we feel that that thing named Wang is truly guilty of heinous crimes; starting with affection and abandoning her at the end, he not only places Miss Lu in what situation, but insults the entire female gender to what extent? If we let it go so easily, not only will Miss Lu be unable to swallow this grievance, but for the sake of the safety of the entire female gender, we also feel indignant.

"Chicken skin cannot be patched onto a duck's body". The result of negotiation definitely cannot allow Miss Lu to once again enjoy happy circumstances; or, in this stubborn society, the result of publicizing may have repercussions against Miss Lu, we are also aware. But Miss Lu's sacrifice is, after all, a small matter, all the more so, she is already a person bearing wounds. Therefore, we hope Miss Lu to use her already trodden self, for the sake of the entire female's future, to risk a fight to the death with this beast in human skin. Below are two solutions:

Nominally, the current world has progressed and does not allow you to take revenge privately. You should file a lawsuit with the court, at least charge him with the crime of "causing someone to mistakenly believe there is a marital relationship and allowing him to commit adultery." Sentence him to three or four years of imprisonment.

Because the world's progress is merely nominal; the result of the lawsuit may not be satisfactory. At that time, it is society that owes you, you should rise up to exercise "the right of self-rescue." Seize an opportunity to confront him with blades in hand. In order to vent this grievance, in order to let out the breath for the entire female gender, any sacrifice is worth it.

Publication of Bao Jiatu's "History of Social Thought" translated version. The translator, Mr. Chen Tingrui, in view of the general need and the lack of works on the history of social thought, has specifically translated Bao Jiatu's great work "History of Social Thought" for researchers of social science to use as a reference. The translator has now published the first half, distributed by the Author's Publishing House. Its contents include (1) the nature of social thought, (2) primitive social thought, (3) social thought of ancient culture, (4) social thought of the Hebrews, (5) Plato and Greek social thought, (6) Aristotle, (7) Roman social thought, (8) early Christian social thought, (9) medieval social thought, (10) Utopian social thought, (11) individualistic social thought, (12) Malthus's population theory, (13) Comte's experimental social thought, and (14) Marx and the socialist social thought. The entire volume contains more than 100,000 words. The language is clear and the translation is smooth. It is an indispensable reference book for beginners in social science.

Film Special

"The Art of Thighs" 215

— Zhu Xian

It's Hollywood's Knocking Brick

It's the Female Star's Family Ability

The new films from Soviet Russia are promoted with the slogan "There are no thighs here, no sex appeal," and surprisingly, during this time of national crisis, when people are feeling drowsy, it serves as a stimulant, seeming to cause a different kind of stimulation. A film without thighs, or even without women, can still be made, but a woman without a pair of shapely, mysterious, and seductive thighs is not popular, especially in Hollywood. The art of thighs "Legart" is something that newly arrived actresses must possess, because when they first arrive, all people can see is their pair of thighs, as for whether they have performing talent, that is the second step. This is the golden rule of Hollywood, and no one can defeat it. Currently, the generally famous actresses, such as Jean Harlow, Marlene Dietrich, Joan Crawford, Helen Twelvetrees, Clara Bow, Nance Carroll, Alice Joyce, Kay Francis, etc., have all passed through this level. Even now they can't give up their family ability, and they must show them off from time to time, showing how a pair of jade legs account for more than half of a woman's body, and is naturally very important.

Marlene Dietrich usually wears men's trousers, covering up her pair of slender, moderate, and well-proportioned thighs, causing many movie fans to feel sorry for her. Mary Pickford also likes to dress in men's clothing, causing her thighs to sigh with the desire to be revealed. But they have already become famous by relying on their thighs, and even though they do this, no newly arrived actress dares to jump out of this range and become famous without relying on their thighs. Now it is said that there is a new actress in Hollywood who claims to break Hollywood's "bad rules," not relying on the sex appeal of her thighs, but to become famous for her acting talent. Whether her revolutionary undertaking will succeed in the future is still uncertain, but the difficulty of her advancement is probably ten times that of others.

"The Art of Thighs" is also a special skill of photographers. Every new actress, after signing a contract, is immediately led to a photo studio, where all parts of her body are photographed in various ways. One purpose is to enable the director to decide how to shoot her figure and attitude in the film, and the other purpose is that these photos can be distributed to newspaper reporters as the best publicity material. Of course, photos of thighs are most welcomed by newspapers. When photographers take photos, they must also use their ingenuity greatly. Thighs that are slightly fat or slightly thin can be made perfect by using the position, direction, and lighting arrangement, as well as post-processing. This is also a kind of "Art of Thighs."

Film Review

Talking About "The Return of the Sword" Again 216

— Ying

The films recently shown by Guotai are purely romance dramas. Their styles are all good, often displaying considerable "reason" and "righteousness," and perhaps also carrying a part of "ethics." It is clear that this is the progress of the American screenwriters' thinking, as they have already realized the mistakes of previously shooting blind love dramas of "money" and "lust."

The story of "The Return of the Sword" is the beginning of a quadrilateral love, but it ends with a triangular love. Such a seemingly complete but not complete ending is naturally likely to cause unhappiness among some viewers. In fact, such an ending adds much poetry and increases a lot of aftertaste.

There is not much to talk about in terms of the theme. Anyway, the director and screenwriter are quite clever. Of course, there should be many things that can be put in the main drama before the entire film unfolds and after the ending, but we know that this is not an easy task. So they straightforwardly cut off the beginning and end, making it a poetic work. From the beginning of the young couple's discord to the departure of her later husband from the United States, everything about how the young couple got together, why they were discordant, and what the ending of the two men and one woman was is not shown. Indeed, if it were shown, one careless mistake could contradict the original drama and cause a big mistake. So rather than praising their high skills and unconventional thinking, it is better to say that they are good at taking shortcuts. But in terms of art, this kind of taking shortcuts is meritorious and well-intentioned.

Speaking of technology, Gold Country's films have always maintained the world's highest honor for photography, lighting, set design, sound recording, and everything else. This film is no exception. The editing is also good. Although there are some disconnections in it, they are not major flaws. There is a little too much dialogue, but it is a film with the beginning and end cut off. If there were even less dialogue, it would be even more inexplicable.

"White Gold Dragon" Was Not Disapproved 217

— Pei Yuan

The day before yesterday (the 7th), this publication carried a major work by Hacker Feng Jun: "White Gold Dragon" Was Not Approved. According to this news, it was indeed a rumor. The film "White Gold Dragon" was inspected by the Film Censorship Board on the 6th. Because the dialogue in the film was a mixture of Shanghai and Cantonese, and most of the committee members were from Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and other provinces, they had difficulty understanding the Cantonese dialogue. Therefore, it was decided to submit it to the general meeting for discussion, and the Tianyi Company, which submitted the film, was asked to provide the dialogue and lyrics of the film for clarification. Therefore, whether "White Gold Dragon" is approved or not will only be confirmed after the general meeting decides. However, we have seen that the "Lost Love" film of the Star Film Company also uses both Shanghai and Cantonese, and it did not encounter difficulties from the Film Censorship Board, so I think "White Gold Dragon" will definitely not be disapproved either.

As for the performance, perhaps Ruth Chatterton's portrayal of the abandoned wife in "Laughing Lady" left us with too good an impression, so this time we felt she was not as good as before. However, in this film, her understated performance is very fitting. The supporting actors Battle Davis and George Brent, one playing a lively and romantic youth, and the other playing a thorough gentleman, are both perfect.

Finally, I want to say that the translated title of this film is very good. The original title cannot summarize the plot and the color of golden assets is too heavy! So heavy that it loses its meaning.

Regarding the Two-Seater Eastern Car in the Film "Madame Butterfly" 218

— Li Yuan

Editor:

I was born in Japan. I spent more than ten years there in my childhood. However, I have not carefully studied the history and customs of that country. Of course, I am not a Japan expert. However, when I was a child, when I was happy, I would also watch Japanese movies, stage plays, ancient plays, etc. I have also seen the stage play "Madame Butterfly", but there was no Eastern car that was a two-seater.

Based on the current situation, Japanese Eastern cars are even narrower than Shanghai rickshaws. It is impossible for two people to sit together. Even if they wanted to, the police would interfere. If two burly Westerners were to sit together, it would be even more impossible.

What I know is what I have observed daily, which is only a small part of the reality. Now that the editor has asked Mr. Ling He to reply based on the facts, let us wait quietly for Mr. Ling's reply.

Reply and Statement 219

— Ling He

－Regarding "Madame Butterfly" and "Asian Storm"

Mr. Li Yuan raised several questions about "Madame Butterfly" in this publication a few days ago. Because the editor wants me to reply, I will reply to the best of my knowledge as follows:

It is true that there are no rickshaws in Japan that two people can sit in, and Westerners certainly do not have this privilege. Of course, this is because the author of the film does not know much about Japanese customs. Not only that, but also in the film, the master calls the maid by her last name (Suau) instead of her first name, which should be a transliteration of the Japanese "Suzuki" or "Sasaki". This is also not in accordance with Japanese customs. Perhaps there are other oversights, but I can't remember them for the moment.

In the article "Review of Asian Storm", a few sentences in the first paragraph were completely printed in reverse order. Now, in order to avoid misunderstandings, I will copy a few sentences from the original manuscript as far as I can remember:

"...Secondly, this film was once translated as "National Soul", which was even remade with the content changed, and a flag with a blue sky and a white sun was added at the end. However, is this not the revival of "National Soul" now?"

This means that the national flag was added to the previous "National Soul", not the current "Asian Storm".

— Pei Yuan

Due to Filming in the Rain

The Tianyi Company recently filmed a "Vitality", directed by Shao Zuiweng himself, starring Chen Yumei, and co-starring Lu Lixia, Yuan Meiyun, and Zhang Zhenduo. It is now known that the film was completed a few days ago, and the first half was privately screened in the Shanxi Grand Theatre. However, although the film has been successfully completed, it has suffered the leading actress Chen Yumei, who fell ill due to overwork in filming this "Vitality". Because the last few scenes of "Vitality" were all rain scenes with heavy rain, Chen Yumei had to run back and forth in the rain, and the plot of the play was in the summer, so she only wore a thin long coat. In this chilly spring weather, wearing a thin coat is already unbearable, and at the same time, cold water has to be sprinkled on the body, so it is no wonder that she fell ill.

Film Novel Desire Tarakanova (1) 222

— Plum Blossom

The time is 1762, after Catherine II deposed the Russian Emperor Peter III and established herself as empress.

This wise and talented woman felt that the incompetent Peter III was not capable of dealing with strong neighbors such as Turkey and Poland for the sake of the country's destiny. After ascending the throne, she used her talents, and Turkey was defeated, and Poland was divided, but she suddenly felt an indescribable depression. Ah, an empty depression, she only felt that the young and beautiful Count Orlov was lovable! For this reason, the court was filled with hostility towards her and opposition to her, especially Count Shuvalov, who was Orlov's enemy. Of course, he had a lot of resentment and jealousy towards Orlov's favor. So the conspiracy to overthrow Catherine was underway, and the assassination plot of Orlov was being planned. The palace was filled with a solemn atmosphere, but in another world it was quiet and pitiful.

"Dong, dong...dong!..." The bells in the monastery, dragging out long tones, played a cold and lonely sorrow in the quiet air; the cold and beautiful Princess Posoti spent such a miserable day, she forgot this lively world, disappointed her beautiful youth, she, resignedly recited scriptures and prayed in the monastery, who knows that she is a princess, who knows that she is the daughter of Empress Elizabeth Petrovna!

Although no one knows, the disgraced Count Shuvalov is an exception: because he knew about this person, and once, carrying a heart full of hope, he secretly sneaked into the monastery, and said to Bodi in a serious and earnest manner, "You, you are the daughter of Empress Elizabeth, this whole Russian Empire belongs to you, get up, overthrow Catherine, we will all support you." But Bodi's heart, like the water in an ancient well, will never ripple again!

Catherine was a resourceful woman. She felt that the people in the country had a very serious attitude towards her, and, moreover, she and Orlov should not let their affair become an open secret, so she summoned Count Orlov to the palace and asked him to lead the army to the front line to conquer Turkey: although she felt a little uncomfortable in her heart, when she thought of the danger of her position, she had to say goodbye to him with tears in her eyes. New News About the "Double-耐克勞夫" Diesel Engine 224

Succinct Study Declares Success

This season's diesel engine types are complete and all-inclusive. The largest is a six-cylinder, seventy-five horsepower, turning one thousand times per minute. When the horsepower is increased to one hundred and twenty, the maximum speed can reach one thousand six hundred times per minute.

The smallest of its engines is nine horsepower. Among its new products, this is the most interesting. Among the several most popular styles of "Double-耐克勞夫", there is one that is small and easy to use, called "Pocket Style". This smallest diesel engine is similar to its mother.

The cylinder diameter is four inches and the stroke is six inches. Generally speaking, the suction cylinder is equipped with a flexible valve, pressure gauge, and automatic filter.

The needle valve injector is installed upright in the cylinder head and sprays into the spherical combustion chamber. The combustion chamber is connected to the cylinder by a single hole. Its structure has undergone many tests.

Equipped with a 皮耐氏 fuel suction cylinder and injector. The suction cylinder is on the frame on the left side of the engine and is pushed by a cam. A spring piston is placed next to the suction cylinder. The intention is to prepare the fuel pipe route before starting.

The machine is started manually at the front end of the engine. The gear that reduces the compression pressure is installed on the exhaust valve, so that the engine rotates several times until the momentum is sufficient. Then, move the lever to fully open the pressure, and the machine will start accordingly. In terms of its 17.5 to 1 compression ratio, starting the machine can often be stable and worry-free. However, in order to prevent accidents, a safety device for starting the machine is also installed. The average effective pressure of the engine is eighty-four pounds per square inch.

The total weight of the engine is about nine hundred pounds. The factory's Shanghai branch (Chinese name 固敏洋行) is located at No. 3 Guangdong Road, this city, Dalaifangzi. Those from all walks of life who want to purchase the above engine will be given special discounts on the price.

The Characteristics of the Ten Horsepower Four-Cylinder Sedan New Citroen Car 225

丨Exquisite Manufacturing, Spacious and Comfortable丨

There are many styles and types of new Citroen cars. The ten-horsepower Citroen is one of them. This is a four-cylinder product. It has excellent construction and is extremely exquisite, so it has attracted the widespread attention of the general public. This type of vehicle is currently being mass-produced by the Citroen factory to meet the enthusiastic demand from all over the world. In order to understand the detailed situation of this product, the reporter recently participated in a test drive. Although this product is named Citroen ten-horsepower, in fact, its spaciousness and grandeur are beyond the reach of ordinary ten-horsepower models. Its wheelbase reaches eight feet ten and a quarter inches, so the assembled car body is naturally more spacious. The sedan body is meticulously constructed with a single piece of steel and is supported by a particularly strong chassis frame, so it is extremely solid and durable. Even when driving at the highest speed on dilapidated road surfaces, there is no worry of rattling. The reason why the new Citroen ten-horsepower car runs so quietly has its own reasons. In addition to the above point, another reason is the special cushion frame of the engine. The method of its implementation is completely based on the principle of buoyancy, so the weight of the engine gearbox part is almost entirely borne by two points insulated by rubber. These two points, one is placed behind the gearbox, and the other is supported by the "A"-shaped horizontal frame in front of the cylinder block. This entire part of the engine is absolutely quiet and has no vibration, and it is worthy of being a great advancement and success in modern mechanical engineering.

The harmonic gearbox with silent two-speed gears is another prominent feature of the Citroen ten-horsepower model. Only with this device is the adjustment and shifting easier, and Citroen's ease of use and natural handling are the natural result. In addition, the spring equipment with hydraulic shock absorbers is also one of its major features. Its quality is excellent and its effect is great, so that drivers and passengers can feel unparalleled pleasure and comfort.

The engine system of the Citroen straight ten-horsepower new car is simple and effective. Its foot pedal and hand lever are both connected to the central main horizontal axis. This kind of engine is not only extremely sensitive and natural in its movements, but also its great storage capacity of braking force is even more outstanding and incomparable. The four-cylinder engine is a side-valve type, with a bore of 68 mm and a stroke of 100 mm. It is connected to the harmonic gearbox by a popular coupling. The steel body is strong and excellent. Its few joints are welded together as one, seamless, just like a whole piece. The chassis frame is particularly solid, so they complement each other and are extremely beautiful and perfect. In short, this new Citroen ten-horsepower product is not only far superior to ordinary so-called ten-horsepower cars, but also truly opens a new era in the automotive industry. "Fu"

Amazing American Car Accident Cases 226

－More Than 29,000 People Died Under Cars Last Year－

Excessive Car Speed is Most Likely to Cause Accidents

Pedestrians Who Are Not Careful Are Also Likely to Lose Their Lives

The main causes of American car accidents in 1932 are approximately the following: driving at excessive speeds, driving on the wrong side of the road, and passing without the right of way. All of the above-mentioned actions of drivers caused 16,000 Americans to die under cars and more than 535,000 to be injured last year. All of the above are from the statistics and analysis made by the American Travelers Insurance Company. Last year, there were 745,300 car accidents, 29,000 deaths, and 904,800 injuries. According to other statistics, 29,500 people died under cars.

According to the booklet "If You Call Us Civilized" published by the American Travelers Insurance Company, car accidents are roughly divided into nine categories. Now, the number of accidents is listed in order as follows.

Cause of Accident Accidents

Exceeding the speed limit 150,050

No right of way 146,500

Driving on the wrong side of the road 81,180

Driving off the road 61,590

No signal or improper signal 52,770

Robbing 24,610

Passing on the wrong side 10,340

Turning or climbing 7,350

Passing a stopped streetcar 4,410

The book also states that the occurrence of these accidents is indeed inexcusable because the driver is driving too fast. In addition, driving in the wrong direction, reckless driving, etc. are all sufficient to cause a tragedy. In short, the recklessness of the driver is the origin of all accidents. However, if this type of driver does not pay attention in time, they will inevitably suffer the consequences one day.

Now, let us further describe the situation of car accidents affecting pedestrians. In 1932, 12,770 pedestrians died in car accidents and 267,280 were injured. The situation of the disaster is roughly as follows:

Crossing at an intersection Accidents

With a signal 11,930

Violating the signal 33,940

No signal 41,610

Walking diagonally 3,470

Crossing between intersections 74,720

Getting on or off a streetcar 3,420

Standing in a safe place in the road 950

Getting on and off other vehicles 3,840

Children playing in the road 43,550

Working in the road 5,680

Riding in a car or hitting a car 5,320

Walking out from behind a parked car 30,780

Walking on the road in the field 10,110

Last year, the number of pedestrians who lost their lives in car accidents was greater than in the previous year. Therefore, it is particularly pessimistic to seek mutual responsibility between pedestrians and drivers in order to reduce accidents. According to statistics, pedestrians who lost their lives due to crossing the road in violation of the signal, walking diagonally, or walking out from behind a parked car accounted for 47% of the total. The book does not want to agree with what the National Safety Council said, that since 1931, fatal car accidents have been reduced by 13.5%, which shows that the public's use of roads has been safer. According to the Travelers Insurance Company, Americans' use of roads in 1932 did not show that they had been safe due to the reduction in deaths. The book says, "Although the total number of deaths this year was 29,000, compared to 33,500 in 1931, the number of deaths or injuries per accident has actually increased. The decrease in the number of deaths cannot be compared with the percentage decrease in the number of accidents. These facts are all stated in the records of each major state. Therefore, in 1932, the mortality rate per accident increased by 1.3%, and the combination of deaths and injuries increased by 2.4% per accident. Although fatal car accidents have been reduced by 13.5%, car registration and car fuel sales have also decreased by 8% and 7% respectively. The reduction of these three items is actually due to the impact of the economic recession and should not be said to be "the public's use of roads has been more alert than before." Now let us compare the situation in 1928. At that time, the number of car registrations was approximately 24,493,000, which is similar to last year's 24,276,000. However, the number of car accidents was 1,400 fewer, approximately 5% less. As for the consumption of gasoline last year, it was more than in 1928, but this is also not enough to say that the distance traveled by private cars last year was more than that of cars in 1928. The reason for the large consumption of gasoline is that the number of registered trucks and buses last year was greater than that of four years ago. In addition, the use of old cars on the roads last year was widespread, and their gasoline consumption was also greater. Another reason is that the number of car cylinders in the market has increased, and their driving speed has also increased. All of these are clear evidence of increased gasoline consumption.

In 1932, due to fewer cars on the market, the accidents of two cars colliding and hitting people were fewer than in 19
